Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais .iij. a cop.	And therefore are cauteries easier to do, because you make them .iiij. times.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	After that, anoint the patient on his back and sides;Et si tu vois que li malaide s’esvaigne et ne revien por le cautere, et qu’
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	And if you see that the illness is relieved and does not return due to the cautery, then gently lift the scrotum with the fingers of your left hand;et qu’il teneit ains lieve li testikels sel
et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	and if the joint is dislocated within, heat the cautery which has two prongs like a needle here is the shape:
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	and cauterize the skin until it pierces all the way through, and you will feel the heat of the cautery with three cauteries;
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	and for this cautery is made with a cautery which has three prongs, so that there are six cauterizations;
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	and the nerve is like the subtlety of a tent and this is the shape of the cautery which has three prongs:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce .i. nerf por coi il i a .viij. cauteres.	And sometimes it is placed upon this one nerve, because there are eight cauteries on it.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	Afterwards, put on the cautery with crushed pepper with honey;
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	Afterwards, let the patient rest and do not move the limb for a long time until he is fully healed.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	And if it is dislocated above, then little will happen; therefore, perform the cautery on the thick part of the cautery needle, or a lot of cauteries by pricking.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and moisture is removed and the patient is healed.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When coldness and much moisture enter the stomach and draw it out of its natural state, and when there are many cathartics in him, and he is not helped by usual remedies and treatments, then the patient should be made to lie on his back and extend his legs and arms.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	Then afterwards, make three cauteries one below the heel of the foot by the amount of a bean, all around the clavicle, and two cauteries on either side so that the shape of the cauterizations is triangular, and there is an equal distance between them so that they are not joined together when they grow pus;
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	and let the cautery be so deep that it pierces both parts of the heart, and let the shape of the cauteries follow this form without adjustment:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	And if you wish to cauterize a large cautery within the stomach according to this form:
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	and whoever is afraid of this cautery, cauterize a small point and sign on the stomach according to the amount you wish to cauterize:
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	then cauterize with all the cautery that is called "points.
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of the disease that we have mentioned earlier, until it is healed.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	When the liver hurts from cold and moisture and from excessive flatulence as it has been moved from its natural complexional position:
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	and the disease is cured by what we have said in divisions, and if it does not help, then the patient should be bled from his finger;
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	and sign within three cauteries according to this form and shape and quantity on the liver, avoiding the hypogastric region where the gut of man comes from;
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	and there should be the thickness of a thumb between each cautery;
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	and the cauteries should be held gently and not pressed too hard on the body;
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	and let half of the cautery burn, and let the patient lie straight on his back with his feet elevated;
et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais;	and if he cannot, then let him lie down, and stretch out his legs and raise his hips;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the procedure:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	And if you wish to cauterize with the steel, be skillful and wise in the art, and beware of burning the entire body, for you would cause the whole body to dry up.
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	And let it come just to a boil, for the skin is very delicate in that place, and you can tell by looking.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	When there is an abscess in the liver, and you want to know if it is in the flesh of the liver or in the membrane:
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	if he is in a cart, let the patient feel pain not too strongly;
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	and if he is on the ground, then let him feel acute pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	And then when this treatment has been applied to the ulcers, the patient should be laid down with his head elevated;
et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	and then sign with oil on the site of the abscess, and then heat the cautery which is shaped like a rod, by which the form [of the cautery] is made:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers;	And cauterize with the cautery until the ulcer is burned, and go down to the bone, until all of the pustules are gone;
aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	after the treatment according to the treatment with bandages until it is healed;
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	and no one should use this cautery except for those who have studied the art of medicine for a long time, and through whom these diseases have sometimes deteriorated.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore he can work boldly, and in any case I think it is better to let him do so.
dou cautere de pleuresin	with the cautery of phlegmon
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one must do cautery to a ulcer with roots of aristolochia, and in such a way:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	take a root of aristolochia that is long, the largest you can find, and dry, and as thick and as long as your finger;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and moisten it in oil, and burn it on a cautery between the throat and neck, and two smaller cauteries slightly lower down on the part which is underneath the beard;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	and two cauteries between the fifth and sixth ribs, declining slightly backwards;
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and one cautery in the armpit, and one over the stomach, and one between the shoulders, and two as you go down from the armpit away from the cautery that is between the shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press your hand at all, but do it smoothly as when applying perfume.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And some ancients said that someone should use a fire cautery like a razor, heat it and place it between the ribs until it reaches that abscess.
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and jump to avoid the pain, as we have said about the liver abscess.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this procedure there is fear of death for the patient, or a fistula occurs that cannot be healed.And some say that if one uses an iron cautery like a razor and cauterizes between the ribs, it will reach the heart; and sometimes pus flows out and the patient recovers, as we have seen happen.
de la mice	of the mouse
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent .iij. manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the illness of the moon as we have said in the divisions of treatments, and it does not help at all, then they rely on three methods of cautery which are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of these, one method is to make three cauteries, or four, by lining up according to the length of the mouse, according to the shape of the liver cautery which we mentioned earlier;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and let the patient be careful on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another way to cauterize is to heat the cautery which has two prongs, as we have shown in the shoulder dislocation;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and gently lift the skin where the mouse is, or the side of the patient's body from which the arrow came towards the left, and let the elevation be according to the skin, according to the length of the body, and the cautery according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After I tie the two nerves inflamed so that the heart is pierced from the other side, and then I draw out the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see, cauterize with all the cautery on three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the scrofula has been cured for a long time, it is better than any of the other remedies mentioned above.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is no good for an idropic, except in the manner that is called "asclytes.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you cure it according to the methods we have described in parts, and your treatment does not help, then you should do four cauterizations around the armpit, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the breast, two behind the back on the spine, and one on the buttock;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cautery be close to the spine of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open for a long time, and do not stop the treatment of the malady after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will hasten, and the two intentions will come together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly is the clave that we have shown before;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and those for the back are olive-shaped, as shown earlier.
de l’enfleure des piez	of swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical and filled with yellow water, you should cauterize on the back of the foot between the little toe and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and move your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	Nor enter too deeply, as they say against the yellow awl, and let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After that, make two cauteries on each leg, at the tip of the tibia;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cautery be long, one below the knee in front and the other above, in the middle of the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauteries untouched for a long time without healing, until the water comes out;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after that, do the other cauteries that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a person has abdominal distension caused by coldness and moisture, and the retaining and digestive functions of the stomach and intestines are impaired and cannot be healed through other means of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering greatly and with great virtue, then make the large cautery on the stomach according to what he has spoken of before about the cautery of the stomach, make the cautery circular;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and 4 cauteries around the body subtly throughout all the cauterization ключ, and 2 cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundance of moisture and the patient suffering, then make cauteries on the elbow, and one cautery on each shoulder, and two small cauteries on the stomach below the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good support.
de la cure des emorroydes	on the treatment of hemorrhoids:
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are in the rectum, one or more, and they are old and consist of large cold and moist corrupted humors, and are treated as we have said with division, but it does not help, then make cauteries:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	3 on the spine of the back, that which is entirely under the armpit, poke and poke little by little in a triangle shape, and 2 cauteries under the body on both sides;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think his stomach is cooled and the meat does not cook, and one sees swelling in the face, then make the large cautery on the stomach as it is said before, and another on the liver, and another on the heart throughout all the cauterization ключ;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cautery remain uncovered for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After curing the area until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshiness which is called "thelul"
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you apply to the ulcer, heat the cautery until it is like a razor, and then place it firmly on the ulcer;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and hold your hand steady so that the cautery comes to the base of the vein, causing the blood to clot;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is a lot of ulceration, cauterize each one as we have described;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after treating the ulcers, apply healing ointments until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery on an abscess, it will bring more relief.
de plaie mal curee	of a badly cured wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure cutting or opening, which we will discuss in its place, such an illness comes that it cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When a fistula occurs, and there is suppuration and a discharge of rotten moisture, you should examine it thoroughly with a thin needle, and be mindful to probe as deep as the tent goes.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the cautery until it is like a razor, insert it into the fistula according to how deep the wound is, and then reheat the cautery as needed until the affected flesh is burnt, once, or twice or thrice, depending on the amount of tissue involved;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and beware of burning the nerves which are within it, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistulas go to the bladder and intestines, beware of those places, and do not make fires too hot, and think that they are not dead;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	afterward cleanse the place until it is healed, and if the wound is sore and the matter has been discharged for a long time, then know that the wound is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter is not discharged, know that the wound is piercing and corrupting the bone at its depth;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus with one of those we will mention in their place.
de la maladie des reins	of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When cold pain comes with wind and does not take the woman's desire, then you must make a cautery on both sides of the back with the hot iron we mentioned earlier;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize it with milk, it will have three cauteries in a line, and they will be of greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then he should be cauterized in the part above the bladder, where the hairs of the pubic hairline begin, on the right and on the left, and each cautery should be as long as a thumb;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and he is cauterized on the back, where there are two cauteries if you need them;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and the cauteries are claved according to the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the bones
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the womb is cold and moist, and does not leave one hopeful of conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their terms delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, they feel great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then you must make three cauteries around the wound, as we have said in the cautery for the bladder, and two cauteries on the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cautery be performed with a key, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the box of the hip and because of this it moves out of its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and if the dislocation is found in the hip joint, then you must cauterize the patient on the hip joint with a cautery resembling a circle, and sign before the place around the joint as it turns, so that the joint is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and let the cautery be performed like those by which one cauterizes the stomach.Quant la boiste de la hainche est disalote, si covient que tu disloques les cuisses,
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present, then make three great olive cauteries, and let the cauteries be as deep as all the warts.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and cure it until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of hip pain
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the hip socket, and it is from coldness and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we have said in the division and the treatment does not help, and the illness is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then you must purge the patient of the gross humors with smelly pills, or other good-smelling pills alike.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After that, make a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the way of making the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, together with burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery has many methods, one of which is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize upon the bone of the hip three cauteries triangularly according to this form, and make them deep and large, and let there be between each cautery a space the thickness of a finger, and let the cauteries be olivary;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes one cautery is made in the middle upon the head of the hip, according to this form: there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you wish, cauterize with the circular cautery which we mentioned earlier in the dislocation of the hip;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circles contain the whole hip, and all the thickness of the flesh is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method done in sciatica, when the pain stays in the hip and does not reach the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes to the thigh and leg, make two cauteries where the patient says the pain is, and one cautery above the ankle, four fingers, on the left side a little;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cautery be with a hot iron, and burn the thickness of the skin;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the pain extends to the sole of the foot or near it, then he should be cauterized where he feels the pain for three or four points with the cautery called 'points'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, have him cauterized more;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if he feels that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then have him cauterized with a hot iron or circular cautery; and be very careful in all your cauterizations not to leave the iron on so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who had cautery done on the ankle of the foot, and they left it until the leg was all swollen, and the foot as well, and it was pierced and corrupted all through the foot.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach ache from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two places together, do cautery in one and the other according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And for the cautery of the hip, from which there is this method, make an iron as thick at the tip as a thumb, or a little less, and pierce it with holes in between so that the distance between them is the thickness of a thumb joint;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and have the hinges of two parts, and also like nuts, and let there be one handle of well-made iron;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And it should be heated until it is bright red and dripping with fat, and then placed on the box of the sick hip, and turned onto the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and the cautery is used once, and left for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make an ointment of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment with ointment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use this cautery sparingly because of its appearance, and we see few who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and yet it is a good cautery, which can be endured by those to whom it is applied.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of medicine burns when you make the instrument to cross between in such a way that the rim of the door descends, and it is made of brass or iron with one side long, and in its height there are two inches, and between each there is the quantity of the thickness of a finger.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they are open beneath and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the box of the hip on the patient lying on his sound side, and then press your hand strongly on the box of the hip.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After that pour between the two circles of the hot iron which has been heated in the fire for a little while, and let the patient endure the heat and burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For he will experience biting just as from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the biting is passed, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip gently, and let it be so for three days, and apply butter as long as that which is black from the burning is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him for three days until the pus drains out;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final treatment after the dressing of wounds until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that colors like salt according to what you did in the hip joint;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is how the hot color is made, and I have written it in the treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, as much of each, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small hole so that the point of a pin can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put on top of this another well-plumbed pot, and put on top of it an alkali and heat and a gentle color on top, until there are two fingers of powder above the colors which you will have well mixed with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it be thus until the water and pieces fall into the plumbed pot, then take all that color and pour it over heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then there will be much fever, which is administered through various medical procedures and cauteries on other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	Because it does the same harm as fire, and there are other remedies with which one can cauterize the hip, such as thistle honey and anardana fruit mixed with soap.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen relates a cure where a man was cured of hip and sciatic pain, and he praised it highly, saying that no other treatment was used, and that the man was healed in a single instance after this cure was performed, and he bathed as instructed below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And he said in such a way that you apply the litarge powder green and dry, and grind it very finely with a little fat, and place it on the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is, and bandage it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours, and according to the intensity of the disease, not feeling the burn anymore.Et puis tu destrouves le cautere et la lie, et mets autre cautere soubs, et dist a li sain
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then he makes him enter the bath until his body is a little warmed up, and he makes him enter the bed, and the pain will go away completely and he will be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicines after a bloodletting.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's dung, it helps a lot;Et quant li poignet de la hainche est desaloiee et se met le pie soubs li corps, si covient que tu la remettes sus li pie, et si covient
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery must be performed in such a way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lamb's wool and grease it with old oil, and place it on the hollow between the big toe of the foot and the other one called the little toe.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Take dry goat's dung, place it in fire until it becomes charcoal, then put it on wool and leave it until it turns to ash.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	Do this again and again, until you feel it reach the hip and the pain ceases.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	This method of cauterization is called "goat's dung cautery.
de la dolor dou dos	of back pain
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes in the back, whether from sitting or from impact or from excessive discharge, or from similar appearances of expanded cold matter, none of these indications are suitable for cauterization except for that which comes from the diffusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After the patient has been purged of foul humors with fetid pills or similar remedies, draw three lines on their back where the pain is located, and make V cauteries in each line according to the strength and amount that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	The cauteries should be performed using the instrument called a "poke." et li cauteriste doit estre presté de sa main, et li poins doit estre embrezés de l’oil ou
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, make three cauteries or four using the key-shaped cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often affects young children, and the signs of its onset are that they have a tight armpit when they wake up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you will find it in the last spine of the back, and the appearance that comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you cure it, then cauterize it with the cautery of salt according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the purple cautery equally affects every part of the spine.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, cauterize around the spine with a pointed cautery tool 2 or 3 lines apart, and have the points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Afterwards, heal the area according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply cautery on any area that is swollen and in a state of inflammation which may be affecting nerves.
de la dolor des jointes	There are two types of cautery: one is by fire and the other is by salt. The salt cautery is better; it does not burn the flesh or the bone or the nerve, but is a great remedy for pains that come from the head.
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain is from moistors that are expanded in every member of the body, and when it comes to feet, which the doctor properly calls "podagra," and when it is from a cold cause and does not heal with medicine, then it is healed by cautery in such a way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	make the mouth of cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if it is necessary to prick the sole of the foot, then use the entire cautery tool on the «point.»
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come up to the knees and other joints, which often happens, if you make cautery on each knee three or four times in each part, all over the olive-shaped cautery;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you need to do more, then do it, but don't hold your hand against the skin any longer than necessary so that the heat doesn't scorch.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knee and the back, administer the cautery we mentioned in his chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if there is pain in the hands, make a point around the finger joint two lines away from it;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there is no pain in the fingers, then make a point on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pain comes from the wrists or up to the shoulders, then cauterize each part and treat the patient well and take medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give him good treatment and purge phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rot of the sinus
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When diarrhea comes from anger, and the bowels descend to the testes and this is new, then when you see it being treated, it shouldn't be done that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and let him eat things that loosen the belly so that the feces descend from his belly;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after you make him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to tense his belly so that the navel is pulled in, and bring your fingers to your hips, and sign from under the waist onto the bone of the wrist, and throughout a sign that resembles half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat up the cautery with which this form is made:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and exudes pus.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the bowels to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and the assistant holds his hand so that it does not return;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and well open the thighs for the patient, and put under him a pillow and a servant on the thighs, and another on the feet who holds his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then put the cautery on the sign all around your hand, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, do it again until you reach the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and carefully guard against the boil erupting when you perform the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so that you do not burn yourself;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the patient does not die, or suffer some other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come to the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cautery for children be subtle according to their size, and for larger people also large according to their size;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after 3 days treat the site of the cautery with butter until the scorch is healed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after that treat it with other ointments until it is healed, and let the patient lie on his back for 40 days so that the wound can close properly;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary to keep his bandages on for a long time so that the boil does not emerge when he tries to move around.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wants to stand up, let him use a well-made crutch, and use it for another 40 days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and has good rest, works little and guards against too much drinking and eating, and against speaking too loudly;
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this advice, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say hereafter about the treatment of cutting on his head.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture in the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ulcers come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they are not growing any more, then do the cautery with the fire according to its quantity, and burn the third of the skin;

de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor. de meselerie	of miasma
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Sometimes ulcers are helped by cautery with great relief, especially those diseases that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Now when you see it cauterized, take heed if the disease is in its early stages, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not disappear or remain, and you doubt that the corruption will spread throughout the disease, then make V cauteries on the head:

et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors. de albaras	of alder trees
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the instruments of medicine are of no avail, then cauterize it with a cautery somewhat deeply, according to the quantity of the thick humors, until the whiteness is removed, and its color changed.

li cure de chancre par cautere	the treatment of sores by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When a ulcer comes at its beginning, and you see it stopping, then cauterize it with the cautery that looks like a circle, all around the edge of the ulcer.

et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	but I do not think this is good, because I fear that it may become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have seen this happen more than once.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a more direct thing is that it be cauterized around, with the cautery which is called "circle", as we have said in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot subside

aprés le laisse ensi.	afterwards leave it thus.If you find a wound that is suppurating and has
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	Because it will hasten death.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing all the way through, then heat the cautery tool from which comes the form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of that disease called "adubelati" until the cauteries pierce the skin, and let the cauteries be such that the patient feels them spreading out in such a way that the flow of the pus is relieved.

li cure dou feu par fer	the fire cure by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of illness there is which is called "corroding", and it is nothing other than a melting of the limbs, for it melts the limbs just as fire melts dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you find this disease in a place that can endure cautery with fire, then heat the cauteries small and large, according to what is appropriate for the location of the disease;if you find it in a place that cannot endure cautery with fire, then take the cauteries which are made from iron and stone and which are called  "circles", and heat them, both small and large, as is fitting for the location of the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	after you cauterize it all over until you reach the healthy tissue underneath, and none of the corruption remains, only the healthy tissue is left.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for 3 days, and put on the cauterized spots a poultice with oil until the burns from the fire are healed, and all the corruption is removed.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After that, treat it with ointments that generate heat.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if after 3 days, healthy flesh does not grow back, that is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then begin the cautery again on what remains of the corrupt tissue.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this wound has sometimes been cured by medication instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nonetheless, fire cautery is the greatest help, and I have already described the cure for the medication ague in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of sores that come on the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that through defect a disease called 'clot' according to our understanding arises in the feet, and is a large, faulty thing that blocks the toe.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries for this disease are according to two methods.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	They are: fire cautery and hot water cautery.Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres: cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery should be heated until it is as hot as a feather, and made of good iron to the size that it can pierce the nail on all sides, with thin edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	after putting it all hot on the nail, turn your hand all around the nail until it comes to the bottom of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and leave it thus for three days until pus begins to flow out;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a poultice of wild mallows ground with salt, and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be uprooted by its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the area with a soothing ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are turned the wrong way round in the body, and often happen in hands and feet, then you must treat them with hot water cautery;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is done like this:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take an iron or bronze rod, or a needle, and put it on the nail and the wart, that is to say, warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and put the rod on it so that it cuts all around, then put a little hot water on it, and hold your hand steady, and press your hand as you turn the rod so that its edge comes to the root of the nail, and it can find the hot water deeply enough to reach the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient endure the biting of hot water for a little while.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it thus, and it will pull out by its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another, until you draw out all those who are in the body, then cure them of the wounds that engender pus.
li cure dou trembler	the cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When someone shakes from coldness of the nerves, or from quartan fever, or other, you must make 3 or 4 cauteries on the spine of the back, 1 cautery between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and 1 cautery on the penis, and 1 on the stomach with olive-oil cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	it will cease the shaking and hasten the health from the cold disease.Car les ners tremblent par moistor qui vient de l’estomac, et le feu qui vient del nerverie du dos
des pustules puans	of stinking pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Sometimes they appear as sores on the body, or stinking pustules, that come from large corrupted matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	Indeed, the nerves shake from moisture that comes from the stomach, and fire that comes from the nerve centre in the backSo it is fitting, when they first appear, to make cautery on each tip of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	with a thin cautery wand made from myrtle wood, whose tip is taken up in fire, or with long roots of aristolochia, or with a lens-shaped cautery.Et si est en la teste, si covient que li cauteres soient fitz sus la teste; et s’il tremble de fievre quartaine ou d’autre maladie,
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they cannot grow from thereforth, but the superfluities from which they come are broken, and they are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great bloodlettings from the artery which is cut at the wound that comes from the opposite side, or in the incision of an abscess, or in cauterizing a limb, and in similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is very painful to stanch.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet when this happens to anyone, you must hurry to place your finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it very firmly until the blood is staunched beneath your finger, and no more drips out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then put into the fire several small and large olive-wood cauteries until they are all red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take I, either large or small according to the wound and where the artery is running, and apply the cautery to that vein where you are holding your hand, and keep the cautery there until the blood is staunched.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it bleeds again when you lift your finger from the wound and the cauteries are extinguished, quickly take another of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease doing this one after the other until the blood is staunched.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	And be sure not to burn the nerve that is nearby, and no other harm should come to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood escapes from an artery, one cannot staunch it well by himself when the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods we have described:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	either by cautery, or by extraction when it has not been treated, or by a strong ligature, or by medicines applied that have the power to staunch blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and it should be bound and compressed skillfully.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers a tight bandage or places burning objects on top, or similar things, will not benefit if only a little.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to someone and they do not have any mirrors or remedies at hand, then they should place their index finger on the wound as we have said, and press firmly until it is stretched over the wound and vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move the finger but moisten it with cold water often so that it is very cold until the blood is congealed and swollen and stretched.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries beforehand about what he will need in terms of cautery and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book of wound treatments.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all the illnesses that require fire cautery, or burning remedies, and their origins, and the instruments, causes, forms of cautery;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and have placed in this chapter from the head to the feet, and I will go through this same way in this chapter so that one can more easily find what they are looking for.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And thus as I begin this, it is fitting, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of cauteries, and therefore greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in treating wounds, and in extracting arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to attempt foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if they come from such people who are so accustomed to their illness that they die easily because of the familiarity with their disease and the severity of its nature;Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and from these one must fear.Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu,
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And of these there are those who give their senses to you and say:'When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am drawing";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is desperate.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should not consent to those who come to you with this method, but place greater importance on your honor than your desire. Do not open recklessly but wisely what you are certain of and what you can obtain and heal.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and diagnosis in treating your illnesses to which salvation may be converted;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will aid you to that good reputation, glory, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lord gives you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have outlined this chapter for you in discussing chapter chapters, according to what is before the chapter on cautery, which I have discussed from the head down to the feet, so that you may more easily find what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	from the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often comes to children when they are born, and when the neck is stretched too tightly from the child's head;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it comes from an unknown cause that one does not know about.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and in all those I have seen death hastened;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason, it seems to me that I should divide the treatment into several parts.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	I saw a child whose head was full of water, and whose head swelled up every day so that he could not support it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and he believed that it was water, and this moisture gathered under the bone above the throat, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the treatment is such that if the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should make a large incision in the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture flows out;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see the shape of the spleen:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the fluid is deeper and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see the edges of the head opening in each part, and the water jumps out when you press it with your hand from within, and it does not return to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	Then you must split it open at the top with three cuts according to this method:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, draw out all the moisture forcefully.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After closing up the cuts with bandages and powders, pour in wine and oil and leave it like this for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then remove the stitches and treat the wound with tenting and ointments, allowing the head to heal evenly, and give the patient dry meat from a dry pot until the limb is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is that you look at where the abscess opens, and the gathering of pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	because sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut it then where the abscess opens and the pus gathers, and fill according to what you are able;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and guard against covering the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and let blood flow, so that the patient dies from blood loss and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	from gout
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When someone suffers from a condition called "cataract" in the eyes or elsewhere, and the disease is old, and the treatment of medicine does not help, then the last resort is cautery with which one will cut the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, when you see them covered, have the patient lie on his back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	afterwards, rub the area with a rough cloth until the arteries become visible, then press the patient's neck tightly with the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein beats, and the spots on either side are after the ears, and they are pressed down;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	then sign the spots inwards, then cover one and press with a sharp spatula on both sides until the vein comes to the bone, and this should be done from the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see that, put the spatula under the artery and cut it from above, cutting through as well about two fingers across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let the blood flow continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the touch, then you must measure the amount of space three times, then sign inwards and press until it comes to the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and that which is needed for the blood to flow out is six ounces, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	then look at the wound.
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if there remains a point on the bone where pus does not come out, then open the wound and drain it, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of the emetic
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient vomiting comes, and a sharp catarrh, due to moisture from the tears and heat in the temples and ancient madness and similar things, and he is treated by various methods of medicine and all that does not help him, then we should open the arteries of the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is that the patient should press behind his temples, and listen to the artery that opens in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is not very strong compared to some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is weak, the patient should hold his neck with some cloth, then rub the area with some rough cloth, and wash the area with warm water until the artery opens clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula, which has a flat shape:
