puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then gently cut the skin until you reach the artery, then pull it upwards with tweezers and carefully separate it from the tissues beneath in every part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, then turn it with the hook to the tip of the nail, then cut off that part according to the quantity of the two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, then the sick person's life hangs by a thread.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw out the blood for a third of an inch, up to half an inch. Et s’il vout adobir la croute et la
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, then you must tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread so that pus does not come before the healing of the wound, and let the blood flow naturally.Et s’il vout adobir la croute et la
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut away the excess between the two ties in that same hour, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a hot iron up to the bone until the shoulder is cut through.Et s’il vout adobir la croute et la
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and it is a good treatment, if the patient does not have a fever and is of a hot temperament.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For fire cautery is helpful in drying out moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	therefore it is even more beneficial for moistness.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or, for the extraction of arteries, one must fill the area with old cotton and place it under well-made tents;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when they are removed, they should be treated with dry remedies that promote the formation of scar tissue, and with tents, until they are healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	and if, without cutting the artery as much as you work on it, you hasten to cover it with cautery, then employ the area with vitriol and hold it in your hand so that the blood is staunched;
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have that at hand, then put your finger on the area until the blood congeals, and apply cold water to the area until the bleeding stops, and then press it as necessary;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and that which is more painful and easier to extract the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cutting cautery in two parts, but the cutting should be well-spaced to guard against their heat for a longer time.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the strumenti is too thin, it holds its heat less well.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be a finger's width of space between the two knives, and then when you have cut into both sides, place the hot iron upon it until it reaches the bone, and close the vein in two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they should be spaced far apart between the two shoulders because they are not fused together by this cautery from top to bottom;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes are flowing down the veins that are above the forehead, and no medicine benefits it, and you see the face of the sick person turn red, and feels movement in the forehead as if trembling;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and if they are pale and moist so that the hair of the eyelids has fallen out, and the eyelids are scorched and blistered from the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they called it the "crushed cure" in old French, and it is that you do to the patient who has this disease by making the hair on his forehead, then make three slits on the forehead evenly according to the length of the forehead;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and one of the slits should be about two fingers' width from the bridge of the nose, running down towards the nose, and the other two on either side of the eyelids, and beware of cutting the arteries that are on either side of the eyelids;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	and keep your hand away from the jaw, and each cut should be about three fingers' width apart across the forehead;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and have ready a piece of sponge and plenty of bandages to wipe away the blood, then fill the spatula with two parts of the mixture from which comes the form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision that is on the temple all the way to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and scrape all the skin that is between the two incisions down to the bone, then do likewise from the middle incision to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Then insert into the first incision the instrument called "culter", which is very sharp on one side and smooth on the other, and it is shaped thus:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the knife's edge towards the chest cavity at the heart, and the flat side towards the bone, and push it in until it reaches the median incision.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And close off all the vessels that descend from the head into the eye sockets as far as the incision extends to this one which opens from the brain, and then likewise do so in the middle incision to the other outside;
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	and then draw out blood equally, and express the area for the taken blood;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	then place in each incision a tent of old cotton, and place on top wet bandages soaked in wine and oil and garlic, and be careful that hot abscesses do not come to it;
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and on the third day loosen the bandage, and administer a large quantity of tepid water, then treat it with basilicon ointment mixed with rose oil, and other remedies used for treating wounds, until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	from the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone suffers from acute cataracts, and you see the eyes sunken and small, and the vision weakened, and the eyelids burnt:
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hair falls out, and in the head there is great pain, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	then you may know from these signs that those substances and this cataract come from many veins, and the mother fluid that is in it, is thus.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And you command the patient to turn his head back, then make a large slit in the middle of the forehead, and another from the broad nose.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And begin the incision from the left temple to the right temple, and let it reach to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move the jaw;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is uncovered, he should suck all the blood with a sponge and then open between the two lips of the cut and put in old cotton and linen bandages;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	then he should bind damp cloths soaked in wine and oil over it, and guard against hot abscesses;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	when it is removed, you should rub the bone until pus starts to come out, then clean it with drying substances that cause the pus to dry up.
En teil maniere:	In this way:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	take two parts of chamomile and four parts of cress, and make an ointment out of it;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and administer it to wounds to dry up pus everywhere.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the ear stoppers
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	All that falls from the ears is one of four things:ou bien est de la chair ou de l’os, ou sang ou mukuge, et si doit on regard
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	or grains, or a stone, or similar objects like iron.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	or seed, like peas, beans;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or fluid things like water and garlic and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it falls into the ear, whether stone or other matter that does not adhere to the ear, nor grow in the ear, then put the ear to the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, then distil a little violet oil or oil of sweet fennel, then administer an emetic;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and make him sneeze with incense, and plug his nose when he sneezes, and put cotton wool or cloth around his ears;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and plug the ear from above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Often this treatment works;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not work, then administer an emetic with subtle pincers, in which way there is the following form:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it comes out with the pincers, that's good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, then administer an emetic with the tip of a sharp, small blade;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it does not come out with that, then make a brass needle and put the tip of the needle into the hole in the ear firmly, and stop up around the needle with soft wax so that the wind cannot enter with the needle;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then treat it further, because it often comes out as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come out in this way, then use glue on cotton and put it around the nail.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the glue onto the stone or whatever it is, and pull it out.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it does not come out with all these things that we have said, then split the ear so that pus and fluid can drain, and for a spasm;
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	and the way to split it is that you first make an incision in the head of the patient, and draw blood according to the amount of its strength, then have the patient sit between your hands and turn his ear up, and split a small opening at the root of the ear where the cartilage connects;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and cut it like a moon, as far as you can go to the stone, then suck it energetically with your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and cure it until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there are grains in the wound and it swells, then administer an extractive remedy;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, then administer a thin spatiumile according to this formula:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer an incision on that spot.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this if you think the grains are moist from the moisture of the ear, until you have made many pieces;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with subtle tweezers and with a sucking instrument, as we have said, so that the extraction is gentle.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In acute conditions when fluid drains into the ear, the patient should first sneeze from congestion, and open the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let him lie on that very ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps out because of this, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, take many small stones according to the length of your finger, thin and light, and heat them slightly in fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	And he puts a hollow reed in the patient's ear, and it protrudes from his foot on the other side, and he pierces another stone upon the stone which is in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and he does not cease to pierce from stone to stone until the water flows out entirely, and thus it flows out completely;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you see that he has a reed, and puts one end in the ear, and the other end in fire until the hottest reed is burnt;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	then do the same with other reeds until the water flows out entirely, as we have said for the stone.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In extracting a foreign object from the body, if it is small like a louse or similar, remove it as we have said in the section on division;
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large enough to be felt, apply the forceps for extraction;et se li corps soit grant et pesans, si doit on le lever et le mouvoir tant qu’il soit estrain, car s’il li estran en
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the easiest thing to remove which is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms from the ears, when you treat it as we have said in the section on distillations, and the treatment does not help, then you must look into the ear towards the sun:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	if it appears that there are no worms, then squeeze them with tiny pincers, and if they don't appear, then take the skin where the shape is.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	It is tight below and loose above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And put the thinnest end of an ear pick into the ear according to the amount of suffering of the malady, then suck firmly on the entire skin;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	do this repeatedly until all the worms emerge.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they don't come out, then stop up the ear with cotton as I said in the section on stones;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not protrude as we have said, then administer the distillation that the ancients have tried in the removal of worms, and you will find it in the treatise on distillation.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and if you distill your oils and medicines into the ear with all this equipment, whose form is as follows:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And it should be made of silver or bronze with small holes underneath, and open on top for distillation.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	And to force the distillation into the instrument, use a bronze vessel especially made for this purpose. And if you see fit, take a razor and wrap cotton around the tip.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	Then pour your oil or juice, and whatever you wish from your remedies into the tube, and let the tube be in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	Then put the razor, wrapped in cotton, into the ear and press your hand gently until the oil is distilled into the outer ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and let the patient feel the heat within, and let the distillation be heated over fire so that it is distilled into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and beware that it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the ear stoppers
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	Some children are born without any holes in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and the same thing happens in adults due to wound plugging, or from pus forming inside the ear, and this plugging sometimes occurs deep in the ear, so it cannot be seen;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and sometimes the hole is pushed out, and one can see it clearly.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	When it occurs deep inside, and one cannot see it, it is a sign of poor healing in many cases, and in such cases, you should expose the ear to the sun;
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the wound exposed, then treat it with this spasm:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And it should be sharp and pointed in front and behind, so that it does not cut the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the wound is on the soft flesh of the ear, then hold it with fine pincers and cut it lightly until all the flesh is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the growth is deep in the ear, take a narrow, thin razor and heat it slightly in the fire, then apply it to the body of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel that the patient feels pain when you hear it, pierce lightly and be careful not to cut the nerves of the ear;
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then put a tent into the ear according to the size of the hole, and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.Et li tient legierement tant que l’ointement soit absorbe, et remets le tent, si tant com il ne se blece point.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Hold it lightly until the ointment is absorbed, and remount the tent, so that it does not hurt. Do this every day until the wound is healed, or take a tent and moisten it in rose water, and dust on powdered vitriol;
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear swollen, then you should draw out the tent and move another moist tent made of cerate that is made from rose oil and wax, until the swelling goes down.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal it until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, soak a sponge and cloth in cold water, and apply it to the ear; and use other treatments that stop the bleeding from the distilling veins.
de la char des papieres	of paper charcoal
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	The hair that grows from the ears when they are moist and dry, you should straighten with tweezers and pincers, and cut off the root of a spatumile;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	then put powdered vitriol on the spot.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if there is pus under the skin, then gently cauterize with a lens-shaped cautery, and after the incision the muces come out;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and many times they return, because nothing remains of their roots;
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized by fire, then those roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	of hail
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times come in papers from themselves one thing that looks like gravel in its shape and hardness, and because of this disease is called "hail," and is a gathering of thick moisture on the paper above and below.
li ovraiges est telz:	the works are such:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take care if the hailstone is silent on both sides, and that is an easy thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Then cut it open widely, then scrape off the skin of each part gently, then take it with tweezers, and peel it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you cannot peel it without piercing the paper a little, it will not harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	And if the tear is large, then sew it up, and treat it until it heals;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	And if it is small, do not use much force, for the natural oils will restore it immediately and heal the wound.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the hail is descending inside the ear towards the upper part, then turn the paper upside down, and hold the hail with tweezers, and squeeze it from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is displaced by the incision, that doesn't matter;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the hail is squeezed, then wipe the wound with salt water, and clean the area of any pus until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the fat around the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinch is a grease that forms inside the eyelids of children more than adults, and it causes great pain to them, and they experience catarrh in the mornings, and cannot stand the light of the sun because their tears flow continuously.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And because they sleep with their faces down, and because their eyelids are moist, their eyes become puffy and the appearance of their eyes is covered by the exinch, which causes the eye to water.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the area with your fingers and feel the exinch between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the manner of the operation is such that the patient puts his head on top of yours.
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	Then take a linen cloth and prepare it into a tent in the shape of a circle according to the quantity that contains exudate from each part, then put it over the wound.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	And press with your fingers on either side so that the exudate is collected within the circle.
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	Then cut an opening in the center of the moisture with a spatula, making a slit that is no wider than the wound being drained.
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	And cut through to the skin as deeply as needed until you reach the exudate.
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	In several applications, exudate comes out of the slit, according to the shape of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Therefore, extract it all with your fingers between your thumb and forefinger, rotating your hand from left to right until it is removed.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	and be careful not to cut into the fissure, so that you do not reach all the way to the eye, lest you injure it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the outlet does not open at the beginning of the fissure, then widen the fissure slightly until it appears.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract as we have said, then moisten with rags in vinegar and water, and apply to the site, and extract with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And if there are such men who grind seal and put it on to corrupt that moisture which remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the cure until it is healed.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if there is a hot abscess in that place, then treat it with soothing poultices until it is healed.And if there is a hot abscess in that place, then treat it with soothing poultices until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	of the hair of papers
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow from the paper which are not of their nature, and they become entangled, then they harm the eyes, and bring about various diseases, as with tears accustomed and softening of the papers and membrane, until it becomes a cause of destruction to the eyes;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and there is treatment according to 4 methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	either by cautery with fire, or by medicine applied directly to the eye, or by incision and stitching, or by canes, according to what I will describe.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	You should place the patient's head on your lap, then return the bandage around his eye to your left hand.
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If it is converted, that is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, then you push an needle through the thread above it.
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and cut through the margin of the bandage where the hairs grow next to these hairs and draw the thread above it throughout the bandage and return it to the shaver;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	then they should do the same under the bandage, under the hairs next to them, all the way to the great artery by the ear, until they reach the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then pull the thread out and place a small tent made of cotton and linen under the bandage, then draw a figure on top of the bandage like a mulberry leaf, although the figure should vary depending on how much you want the bandage to rise where it is divided in two.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if it is on a part that requires this, apply a large amount of paper according to how soft the paper is;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	then do the spathanile over the two lines you have marked, and start from the large armpit up to the small one;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and let one of the slits be near the natural hairs in the thickness of a hair root, then plug it with the point of a needle in one of the two corners of the heart, then peel it all off;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then sew the two lips together with a thread of fine woollen yarn, and stop the bleeding, and dry up the excess thread over the two eyelids with any sticky substance, if you see fit to do so;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, don't worry about it and leave the sewing and threads for three or four days;
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then dress the wound without sewing with dry and constricting things, for paper shrinks when the wound is souded and closed, but the stitch is moved (as the ancients say), and this work is done without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	and if there is another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and it is that you sign the paper with a shape that is also like the leaf of myrrh, as we have described it, at 3 inches apart according to the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	then cut out those on top with small scissors evenly according to the shape that is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you do not have the strength to hold the tweezers, and the object is not even, so take a needle or thread, and put it in among the shape.
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	And put another thread through the large artery, and the second thread through the small one, and bring together between your fingers the threads evenly;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly and lift all the skin on which you have signed, as we have described it, then bring together the two lips of the wound by sewing, and dress it until it is healed.
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess comes to your incision, then soothe it with cerate and similar soothing ointments;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes the hair of the paper is converted:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	if you should use what we have said about the incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the stitching in both is more artifical.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of bones is as follows:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and you should convert the paper and cut it inside according to what I have said, then make two bones by art, and two subtle strings as long as the paper and the width of the spathamile is;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut as two heads from both parts where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then assemble one and the other subtly above what rises from the paper of the eye, and strain the two bones from their formed parts;De la dislocation de la teste et de la nuque si est que tu convers le membre en la jointe ains que li chiés ne se desjoignent:
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and let it stay like that for a few days, and the skin that was stretched will die and become hard and fall off as it heals.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes time, if the wound has a lot of pus, then treat the wound until it is healed;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and when the wound is sutured and the paper is lifted, the hairs will no longer grow;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the shape of the two cones that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of length and breadth:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	the work is such that you pierce an aiguille-like needle, and through it thread a silk thread;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	then join the heads and tie them tightly, and the length of the threads should be a palm long;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then place in the socket another short silk thread, and tie the ends of the thread;
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then put the patient's head on your lap;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and with the sun shining on it so that the work is visible, because it is a subtle and fine operation. Then push the needle all the way into the root of the hair, and pierce through the skin gently until you reach the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	then pull out the hair all the way to the root, and put in the socket that hair, if there are 1 or 2 or 3 or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	then pull your hand away so that the hairs grow out through the skin with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the socket is treated and the hair does not come out with it, then you must pull the socket from below all the way to the thread that you have tied there, until the socket comes out through the hole above and you see it with your eye;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	then you will pull out the hair and thread, and close the eye and leave it for two or three days, until the hair grows back in its place and the flesh heals over it;
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	and if the hair is short, accompany it with a long hair from the eyelashes, and let it grow with it until it is elongated and then pull it out.
de la porriture de l’oil	of the eyelash
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease called 'alopecia' or hair loss occurs in the eye, there are two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	one is natural and the other is unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens suddenly from a wound, or a cut, or cautery, and similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way to treat it is to split that sutured skin, and loosen the eyelids, and place linen pads inside, and keep it clean until it heals;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and you must not use in its treatment anything that dries and constricts.Et la seconde maniere est que li poilz de l’oil, li quels sont petis, seche et descuit, et s’en
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the disease will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but work with softening things, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and the rose of water or altée and flaxseed are cooked, and diaquilon oils melted in any oil, and wrapped in a tent, and the cure of this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the treasures of your cure are that you must be careful that it does not harden again according to the form it was before;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and these works that we have said are not strong except as remedies for this disease, so that it does not return according to the form it was before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the flesh that comes in the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease, which is below, is truly called "axacrati", and it is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	Accidents come from wounds and tears and cauterizations and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the way of the work in it is that you pierce a needle with a double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make it pierce from the left eye to the right, so that the threads come out in two places on the body;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then draw the thread through the eye of the needle, and tie it tightly around the spatulum.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the shape of the paper returns according to what is appropriate, that is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	if not, then take a razor and insert it into the slit, and turn the paper over, and make two slits along the side within the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the slits of the two sides be at the two corners of the incision that you have made, and make angles so that when they are assembled, the shape is like the shape of the letter "I" in Greek;
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove that thread, according to the quantity that its sides are sharp underneath, from that which follows the paper; then join together the two separated parts and sew them with a lamb's wool thread;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it according to what we have said about medicaments for softening and tenting, until he is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease comes from a split or a stitch or cautery, then you should make a clean split beneath the hairs of the eyelids, and according to what is mentioned above.
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then remove the tent between the two lips, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and the procedure should be performed according to the form of the disease, because it is very diverse in form, and the wise master prepares an instrument with all his power so that he makes the figure return to its natural form.
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the patient himself, according to what he needs in terms of procedure and instruments, in many different ways.
dou soudement de la papiere	suddenly from the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this soudure happens to men in such a way that the papery eyelid is separated from the white of the eye and cannot move or perform its natural functions, then you must therefore insert the tip of a razor beneath the papery eyelid and gently lift it upward;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and stretch them until you reach the subtle sphincter, which is neither too tight nor too loose, so that the patient can bear it and the eye is not damaged by the sphincter being too tight.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and make your incision on this membrane gently, so that it returns to its natural shape;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and cleanses the entire membrane, and sometimes they make an incision in the eye for pus to drain, and they flush it with clean water and apply a poultice;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then they place a piece of linen between the membrane and the eye, and put a pad soaked in egg yolk over the eye.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after three days, they use an ointment and poultices until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	You should know that there are two types of fingernails:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	one is nervous and similar to hard skin, and the other is not nervous but resembles congealed white moisture; when touched with iron and pinched, it feels nothing.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	and both start towards the large tear duct, and grow little by little until they cover the entire eye and all light and movement.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incision is that the patient should look down at you, then he should open his eyes wide:
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	take the paper in your hand, then use your fingernails like small pincers, and stretch them upwards;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and thread it with horsehair, or cow hair, or bull hair, and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	then pierce the needle all the way through, and tie the hair to the eye with a thread, and stretch it upwards, and scrape along the hairline of the eyelid towards the tear duct with subtlety and gentle force, leaving the natural flesh of the tear duct untouched so that the incision does not cause the flow of tears;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and sometimes the nails come off at the cuticle only, and on the nailbed, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then one scrapes all around the wound, so that this is the shape:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the spatula does not touch the fleshy membrane and break it, and that the nailbed is not pierced;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after making the incision, put a little powdered silver into the eye, and make an eye-patch from lime, and leave it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not sensitive, and you cannot pierce it with a needle, and the cuticle will not go in, this kind of nail is often cured by medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow as I have described in the section on division, and if you see it covered, then treat the eye of the patient, and take the spatula with a small pointed end according to this shape:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And raise the nail gently, and if you see that it does not narrow and the pus is pressing out, then distill from your mouth into the eye a collar made of litharge and red copper ore ground together, and stop up the eye until the next day.
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then start the other work according to this same method, until it is all removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If there is nothing contrary in the eye, such as a hot abscess, then milk it, and first cure the hot abscess until it is healed, then start the work again as before, until it is healed.Si li ungle est ost, adonques tu le remets, et si li est alongie, adonques tu le rompts; car il ne poait demorer a son leu.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh in the eyelid hurts in the eye greatly, then suspend it on a hook, and cut off a portion of it and not all of it so that the body of tears does not come;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	then distill into the eye red collar made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh which grows above the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	In some people's eyes, red bumps sometimes grow, covering the eyeball and sticking to the eyelids, and they look like a rose of marble;
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	and the treatment is for the patient to put his head in the right position, then he works the eyes, and then all that body part into appropriate hooks, and hold it there with strength;
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	then cut the first hair, and go all the way to the root, being careful not to hurt the eye during treatment;
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	and it is done with the knife of the spurge plant that we described in the incision of the nail and with small tools from which one removes the pus, as the form after this chapter demonstrates;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	and when the incision is complete and all the pus removed, then apply the eye of a seal mixed with red colloid and similar corrosive medicines, and place over the eye a cotton pad soaked in egg white so that it is secured from hot abscesses;
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	and if nothing remains and the blood circulates freely, and you doubt a hot abscess, then leave the eye and treat the abscess with things that soothe hot abscesses;
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	then return to your work until it is healed, and thus do as often as the eye is adjusted in this way.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, you should also lighten the treatment of each weak eye in the natural way:
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and in accidental work, with iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not push your hand into any of these works until you see that this member is suffering from that work.
des voines des eulz	of the veins of them
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Thus are red veins which are covered on the eye, and tolerates one's vision and weakens the eye all day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	So it is necessary that you first examine the eye, to see if it is swollen, and if there is no other disease except the swelling;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then treat it in this way:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to put his head in yours, then open those veins all around gently, and let the veins be subtle and doubled according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And let two compresses be in degrees in .i. body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then open those veins forcefully, and draw the blood hour after hour, until you see the veins removed from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and be careful not to harm the eye with the tips of the spatules, and do this work at noon in front of the sun, and be very careful in your work so that you do not poke through those veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, distill into the eye a green and red colloid to corrupt what is left of the ulcer.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot collect all of it in that hour, then make a poultice for the eye from soothing things to alleviate the pain of the eyes, and leave it for several days until the pain is relieved and the hot abscess has settled, then begin again according to the method described above until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And this is how you make the solution:
de la fistule de l’oil	of eye fistula
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The plant called "arissati" milfoil:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you have treated it with cautery and medicine as I have described above, and it is not healed, then cut into the abscess where it should be, and draw out all the moisture until the bone is exposed.Et si li os est touchez et les forces de la fistule se despartent ou s’estengient, si est la fistule sane;
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is uncovered, you will see the corruption and blackness; then examine all the instruments by which this form occurs.
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	It is called "sharp head", and it should be made of iron and sharpened like a file as it appears in this illustration.
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it over the location of the corrupted bone, then twist it between your fingers and press your hand slightly until you feel that the corruption has been removed.
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	And do this several times, then dress the wound with drying medications.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the wound is closed and healing occurs, and the skin of the bowels has healed over a period of 40 days without any bad incidents or relapses, then you may know that it is healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If not, if there is anything else but to bring the fistula back to the opening of the navel according to this illustration:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and you uncover the bone a second time with iron and sharp medicines; and when it is uncovered, it takes on the shape of the iron according to this form, and let the head of the iron be three-pointed and the shaft be tapered to the tip as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	then he puts it on the bone below the eye, and moves his hand away from the eye slightly, then returns to pushing the iron in until it penetrates the bone and the patient feels it through the pressure of the wind if he holds his hand over his nose;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	then restore the area with dry remedies as I have taught you, and when the flesh has grown back and hardened, examine the matter under the nail;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter object to the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	of the exit of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eyes are fully open and there is no disturbance or weakening in the nose, then you must ligature the patient;
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	then let him sweat, then apply cupping glasses or a hot compress without burning to draw out the poison, then put on an ointment made of acacia, aloe, incense, and sarcocolla over the eye, then bind it with bandages and cloth;
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the method of the bandages is that you fold soft cloth several times, then place one on top of the other depending on how much the eye needs;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then tie it tightly with a sturdy bandage and restart the cupping glasses to draw out the poison without burning;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the cupping glasses and leave the eye bound tightly day and night, and if the bandage becomes loose, then you must tie it tightly again;
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the bandage after a day and a night, and if you see the eye healing, that is good;
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	then restart the plaster, bandages, leeches, and cupping until he is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	from a torn woven fabric
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruption comes in the woven fabric, then it opens, and comes out of the paper like a grain of resin, and is terrible to see;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then, if you see it covering, the work is such that you insert a needle into the root of the affected part, just above the elbow joint, then insert another needle where there is a double thread in the arm;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and have it pierced, and leave the first needle according to its position;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cover the double thread and tie a part of the skin around it tightly, then withdraw the needle and put on another wet egg yolk;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and let it be until the thread cuts through the skin, then treat the wound with comforting things until it is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and sometimes the wound is constrained by a cloth wrapped around it on all sides, until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eyes cause great pain, then pierce them with a sharp spathum that comes from within the eye, and dry up the watery albumen and lower the eyes, and enter them immediately.
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then extract it until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the socket of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease called "alcunnati" has no cure except for cow's milk that is collected in the eye, resembling water but not being water;
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the method of treating it is to have the patient sit on a prepared seat and straight, then hold their head with both hands and move it until you see the milk come out from above your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then let him remain thus, and let the light be dimmed and let him see things as he used to;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if they do not go down, know that it is acute, and if the bowels do not move as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	If you make the patient sit between your hands, then take the spatulum and press it gently on the conjunctiva under the cornea and the cornea itself, until the bowels move.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when it is issued, then distill into the eye a warm mixture of honey and water or fenugreek that has been boiled in water, then let it be treated with another remedy until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	of the eye waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have already discussed the signs of acute conditions and how to diagnose them:
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	Now we will discuss treatment according to health status.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You should make the patient sit between your hands with his eyes closed and away from sunlight, then open the healthy eye wide and press it firmly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then put the paper to your left eye if the eyes are left-handed, or to your right eye if they are right-handed;
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	then take in your right hand, if the eyes are left-handed, the instrument called "almagda", or in your left hand, if the eyes are right-handed;
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	then put the tip of the instrument near the edge of the cornea by the thickness of a hair in that white part of the eye where the lesser tear duct is located, then gently push the instrument called "almagda" through, and turn your hand so that almagda enters the empty space; feel for it to reach the hollow:
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and the depth of the path of almagda should be at the bottom of the space between the pupil and the edge of the iris:
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and it is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	you will see the bone through that film due to the clarity of the corneous tissue, then place the instrument where the water is, and then express it below one way after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the pain descends now, then the patient sees before him and the instrument in his eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After rest for a little, and if the water rises back up the second way, force it out with the instrument, and when it is pushed in and does not rise, gently pull out the almagda by turning your hand a little bit at a time;
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	then put in some water with a little sealing wax, and leave the eye inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then, push the eye out with force, using a wet sponge or lamb's wool in rose oil and an abundance of egg white, and bind it with clean cloth.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, put on a mixture of comfrey with an abundance of egg white.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the almgada cannot enter the eye because of its hardness, for there are some people who have very hard eyes, then you must use the instrument called 'albarit', which has this form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And so pierce only the conjunctiva, and do not go too deep, but make the hole small, then insert the almagda, as we have said;et il li covient boire l’oil, et metre dedens un poc de seil gemme por le conseruer, et li covient leure un poc de sang de son corps par la matinie sus la piere et les membres
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and at the completion of the work, prepare the patient for sleep by having him lie on his back in a dark place.
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and he should avoid all movement and eat light foods. He should not move his head to the right or left, and should be bound according to his condition for three days.
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then he should be untied in the same dark place, and his vision tested. He should then be shown some objects, and then have the bandage put back on for seven days.
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	You must not do this during the hour of the cure or after the incision now, but you should lighten it so that the water rises quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If a warm abscess comes, untie the eye before the seventh day, and apply something that soothes abscesses.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	and when it is soothed, then loosen the bandage and place a blindfold over its face to cover any light, and let it be in that dark house.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then exit the house little by little, and return to your senses;
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	and know that no disciple should intervene in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us who was from Spain, who told us that in his land they made a medicine called almagda, which drew out pus, but nevertheless I have never seen anyone in our land make it, nor have I ever read about it in the books of the ancients;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	and perhaps it is a new thing.Et si on le fait, il faut que li homes soit en bon teint et sans

et soient d’arain proprement:	and they should be made of clean iron:Et il faut que li homes qui le fait soit en
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en .iij. angles ague.	And let the heads be of the same subtle metal, and the rear in 3 angles sharp.
de la char sor le neis	of the heart through the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	At times, various deformed children are born, among whom there are some who resemble scorpions at the base of their feet.
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	And if there are any with a fissure in their skin of a red color, and if any have a soft swelling of a white color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	For those with a soft swelling and not a fissure, you should have the patient sit between your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and open his nose, and pour the oil onto those swellings, and draw them out;
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then grasp what you can with a fine spatula on one side, as long as you know that the swelling is completely removed.
