Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if anything remains which cannot be removed, open it with the smallest and thinnest instrument so that nothing remains;
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if without difficulty, or an abscess forms, cut it as it should be;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if it is malignant abscesses, then hasten and cauterize them until the pus is drained and all the putrefaction is removed, then pour cold water or vinegar or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If it works on the nose, and moisture comes up to the palate, you know he's cured;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if moisture does not break through as it should, you know that there is putrefaction in the bone above, and the instruments will not work to cut it out:
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	therefore you should bind a thread of coarse linen around it, and tie it with the fingers of one hand, and between each knot make an interval of a finger or less;
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	and let the patient hold one end of the thread in his hand and pull it through his nose into his mouth;
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and many times children do this at school, and it is an easy thing for anyone who wants to do it;
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	then hold the head that comes through the nose in one hand, and the other head that comes through the mouth in the other hand, and pull them apart one after the other while being careful not to tear the membrane connecting them.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you know that the umbilical cord has been corrupted by the corrupt blood, then cut the cord, wipe away the blood, and wet the cord with Egyptian ointment, and put it back into the nose as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the ointment has corroded all that remains of the flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then put a piece of cotton in the nose for several days until it is healed, and if it needs dry medicines, use them;
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the instrument for purging the head, through which oils and medicines are distilled into the nose:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it is of silver or bronze, resembling an open lamp, like a cane, and lead them as well.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you see fit to make a closed cane, and let the instrument be filled for purging the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it has a handle on the top to hold it when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the heart through the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a disease arises in the head of the new-born, called "telul", which grows and becomes large, until it is a sight to behold;
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	and for this reason you should cut it at the beginning and remove all of its flesh, then place upon it the cautery or burning medicine;
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	and if one delays in cutting it until it has grown large, then take heed whether it is hard, dark-coloured, and lacking sensation:
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	don't touch it with iron, for it is an encrusted abscess; for when one cuts it, great harm comes to the patient;
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	and if the abscess is from a soft touch, not from a pus-filled color, and you see that it can be completely covered, then empty the wound and cover it without fear, and treat the area with dry and constricting substances.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the nose has been cut and sewn up
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when a solution of continuance comes in one of these soft cartilage-like things, it benefits little, unless in some men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	Therefore, when this happens to someone, check if the wound is fresh with all its blood;
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then bring the two lips together with a stitch, then treat it until it is healed;
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	and if the lips are separated on both sides, then you should scrape all the parts of their skin until they heal, then bring the two lips together with a stitch, hold them in place, and apply powdered dragon's blood and ground incense;
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	and place a piece of strong plaster or other binding plaster over the powders, and leave it until it falls off on its own, then treat the wound with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The method of sewing is to assemble the thread:
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or with needles as we have said in the sewing of the belly;
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or with thread, as I have already told you.
des apostemes des levres	of abscesses on the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	In the lips of men there are hard abscesses inside, resembling beans in size, both small and large;
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	therefore you should turn the lips inside out, and split each pustule, and squeeze it with tweezers, and cut into each part;
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	then apply powdered vitriol to the wound after cutting, until the blood is staunched;
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave it with garlic, and clean the area of dry matter until it heals.
de la char des gencives	of gum swelling
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times a hard lump grows on the gums, which the old call 'albulus';
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	you should hold it with tweezers and cut it at its root, and let the pus or blood flow out;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	then put on the spot vitriol powder, or other restraining and drying powders;
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	and if this ulcer returns after the incision, and it happens many times, then the second time, cauterize it:
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	if it does not return after cautery;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the forms of fistulas for covering.
des sordens	of the eyes
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Sometimes they are assembled on the head of teeth, inside the mouth between the gums, scabs which are ugly and rough;et si li dents s’en fuient, si doit aler a leu;
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	and if the teeth escape, then it should be treated; and sometimes the teeth are black and yellow, and green, as far as the corruption comes to the gums, and the teeth stink;et li gencives seche et brulee et trante, si doit aler a leu de cautere et
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	and the gums dry and burned and torn, then it should be cauterized; and you must make the patient hold his head in your hands, and his teeth or sores appear, so that nothing remains;et tu sais que la coper par le chief ou li gencives est aspre et dure, si covient que tu le raines a l’incision ou au cautere.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	and thus do for darkness and greenness and yellowness and other discolorations, as long as they remain.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	and if one removes what is at the first layer, that is good;
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	if not, then recommence on the second day and the third, until you have removed everything;
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	and know that teeth require various instruments for removal, according to what the work demonstrates to you, because the rasors used to remove teeth have other forms than those used to remove between teeth;
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	and these forms and others should be prepared for you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary when you cure a tooth of its pain that you delay drawing it as long as you can, because it should not be done quickly;
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because it is a very sensitive substance until one has no excuse to draw it out.Et si li dent est trop dur et ne peut estre traie, qu’il le fust si boin com il esteuit;
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Therefore, when the patient is compelled to withdraw, you must be certain about the toothache.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain deceives the patient, and he thinks it is in the tooth, and has the good tooth pulled out.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	Yet the pain does not go away because of this, until the bad tooth is extracted, for we have already tried it with these teeth:
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are quite certain of the aching tooth, then you must scrape around the tooth all around, spatulating strongly to push back the gum from all sides;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then you must grab it with your fingers or with fine tweezers in the front and back, so that it is well loosened, then grip the tweezers tightly;
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	And let the patient sit in your lap, holding him steady so he does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	Afterwards, pull out the tooth firmly without breaking it, and if it does not come out, take one of those instruments and insert it into each side gently, and move it as you did before.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	If the tooth is broken and eaten away, then you must fill the holes with cotton, where the holes are;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if they are gently squeezed with tweezers so that they do not break when being squeezed.
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	and it is necessary to work gently around the gum to loosen the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And be careful that you do not break it and leave a part behind, which will cause greater pain due to the root's toxicity.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware that you do not act like unskilled surgeons who, through their hastiness and boldness, sometimes break the jaw, and do not listen to what we have instructed.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but sometimes cause great harm through the roots by their probing, or break the jaw, as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the tooth is pulled, wash the socket with wine or garlic and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and if bleeding occurs, which often happens, apply powdered vitriol to the socket;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if that does not work, cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The probes used to loosen the teeth should have long points and thick shafts so that they do not bend when you pull on the tooth;
et ce sont les formes:	and these are the forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should be of thick members so that they do not bend when pulling, and they should be well-made of iron, and they should be toothed to hold the roots.
de la racine des dens	of the root of teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains in place, you should apply moist cotton on the area for one or two days until it softens, and then use tweezers called "algefri", which make the shoulder look like a bird's beak.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	They should be made smooth inside, just as a file is made, and this is the form:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out with all these tweezers, you must uncover the skin all around the root, and place the instrument called "althali", which is made of ivory, thus its form:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	It should be thick and strong so that it does not break, and if the root slips out through it, that is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If not, use all the instruments, of which the forms come later:et li auter chiés soit en sa place tant com il convient, et li membrez soit adoblez par li tenailles, et li armeciers doit prendre leu de la piere s
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And one should also use this instrument with .ij. tweezers, of which the form is as follows:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other tools which are before in the reason of teeth, and with this instrument that resembles a large pair of tweezers, of which the form is as follows:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And the other shoulder should be in its proper place, and the bones should be pulled together with the tweezers, and the surgeon should take hold of the stone, and the instruments should be strong enough not to break. know that there are many instruments for teeth:et li auter chiés soit en sa place
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other instruments which are not counted;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	and the experienced master surgeon finds by himself his instrument according to what his work and the illness show him, for there are many kinds of illnesses where the ancients did not teach any instrument because of their diversity; and if he does not break or displace a bone in the head or elsewhere, but only probes them, then he searches for the instruments that he needs, which I have told you about, and uses gestures to help himself, by which this is done:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And they should be thick and strong enough to hold the bone so that it does not slip but can be held and removed;
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	then restore the place with suitable medicine, and if there is a protuberance in the bone that is small, then treat it with this instrument:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When a tooth appears not according to the natural order of teeth and its shape is ugly, especially in young girls, then you should know whether the tooth is new after the baby tooth, and it is not in its proper place, and you cannot push it back or file it down;
adonques lou raie;	then cut the hair;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	and if it is airy with the tooth, then take this instrument of which there is the shape, and is similar to a small beak, and be made of tempered iron:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And pull it gently day by day because of the hardness of the tooth and so that you do not move the others; and if it is apparent that it can be filed, then file it with a type of file like this:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	and is also like the liming tool used for making needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	and gently files the tooth a little bit at a time, so that it does not move until it breaks;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	then smooth it at the end to a point, and if the tooth is too sharp and cuts the tongue, then file down the sharpness until it is even, so that it does not cut the tongue or impede speech.
quant li dent lochent	when the tooth is loose
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the front teeth are loose from a blow or from falling, and the patient cannot chew without shitting, and you have tried binding remedies but to no avail;
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	if they need to be restrained with a gold thread, for silver threads turn green and rot, but gold never moves.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and the thread should not be too thin or too thick, according to the quantity of space between the teeth;
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you want to move the teeth, take the thread and wrap it twice between two healthy teeth, then put the tooth between the teeth, whether there is one or more of them, until you reach the healthy tooth on the other side;
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	then restart the coverage until the part where you started, and strain your hand gently and firmly, so that it does not move;
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and make sure it is tied at the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then cut the teeth of the thread with pliers, and join them together, and tie them between the healthy tooth, and place it so that it does not hurt the tongue;
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and then let it remain thus tight as long as it can stay, and if it comes undone, or the threads break, then tighten it with another thread;
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it remains and serves thus throughout its life, and that is the shape of teeth and the arrangement of both healthy teeth and diseased teeth, as you can see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when a tooth falls out, one replaces it in its place, fresh one after another, as we have said;
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and only a wise and experienced person should attempt this, and sometimes one makes a tooth from cow bone, and puts it in the place where there is a deficiency, and tightens it as we have said, and it remains and serves for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	to cover the vein of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Sometimes this ligament which comes under the tongue, where nature is, causes one to be born thus;
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by accident of a wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the treatment is such that you open the mouth of the patient, and hold his head in your hand, and lift his tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then grab the nerve of the jaw, as wide as the tongue is dislodged from its place, and if there is hardness or swelling, and it is a sudden wound, then hook and grab that nerve firmly;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and be careful that the cut is not too deep, for the artery that is underneath;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have finished, raise the area with rose water and garlic, or with cold water, then place under the tongue a tent of linen;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and apply the cautery to the patient every night so that the wound cannot heal.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And if bleeding occurs, put ground vitriol on the area;
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	and if the blood vessels bleed, then cauterize them with a slow-burning cautery, which is good for this.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	then clean it with another cleaning until it is clean,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	and if you see a black or dark-colored sore, or a hard one that the patient does not feel, then do not touch it, for it is gangrene;
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	and if it is inclined towards white, and there is moisture in it, then open it with a sharp instrument, and release it from both sides;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	and if the blood vessels bleed with your treatment, then put powdered vitriol on it until it is stanched, then return to your treatment until you draw out all the poison;
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then lift up the armpit and underarm, and clean it with other cleanings until it is clean.
des apostemes de la gorge	of abscesses in the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	At times, lumps develop in the throat that are called "godath," and they are properly called almonds. And when you treat them as we have said in the division, and they are not healed, be careful:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	if they are hard abscesses of little size and a dusky colour, do not touch them with iron.si son grandes et douces si les incises par petite entors qui te semble qu’ele soit en la maniere d’une fure; et
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if they are large and soft, cut them with a small incision in the manner of a furrow; andif the root is large and red, do not touch it with iron, also for the discharge of blood;si son rouges et li racine est petite si le metes sus un linge qui soit f
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	if they are red and the root is small, place it on a cloth that is folded in four, and leave it until it bursts, then you will separate it or it will burst by itself;et s’il est meurs et l’enflure dure, si le met
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is swollen and the swelling lasts, place it on a clean cloth, and if the abscess is white and the root fine, have the instrument for cauterizing ready, but first check that the abscess is calm and pacified.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then have the patient sit facing the sun, with his head in your lap, and open his mouth and press his tongue down towards all the instruments, from which this form is taken.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	and it should be made of silver or fine brass like a little knife:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	When you press the tongue against all this instrument, and see the abscess, take the needle and thread it through the almond, and draw it out above as much as you can;
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and draw up some of the threads with it, then release the instrument, from which this form is taken, which looks like a forceps;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	and its jaws are curved and one jaw is higher than the other, and they are very sharp, and it is made of iron or steel;
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this instrument available, use a pair of tongs with the same shape:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And it has serrations on one side, and smooth on the other;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and when you have finished with one of the testicles, then finish with the other in the same manner, and after the incision, gargle the patient with warm water, and water and garlic, and if there is bleeding, gargle the patient with water, or cooked pomegranate peels, or myrtle leaves, and similar things, until the bleeding stops.
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then dry it until it is healed;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	sometimes abscesses form in the throat other than the two testicles, so treat them just as the two testicles are treated.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	I treated a woman for an abscess that was inside her throat, namely, one of small size;
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	and her throat was almost entirely closed off, so that the woman could not breathe through the passageway which was blocked, and she could not eat or drink, and would have died in one or two days.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	And the abscess had grown so much that it had forced out two holes in the nose.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I hastened therefore at once, and fixed one hook in his anus, then drew him out violently, and drew out a large portion of bowels.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	Then I inserted another hook into the other nostril, and I opened his mouth and pressed his tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	Afterwards, I inserted the hook into the abscesses, and scraped out a portion of it, and only a little blood came out violently.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And thus the passage of the throat of the woman was cleared, and she began to drink water and then wine, and I did not cease to cut the abscess for a long time;
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the abscess grew again, filling up the place that I had emptied, until it became very large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	Therefore I lanced and cauterized it within the throat:
ensi demora sens croistre;	Thus it stopped growing;
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I depart from these parts, and am but what God made of me after my departure.
de l’uve	from the grape
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When there is swelling in the eye, and it is swollen and long, it is called 'perpendicular'.
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it is below, large and round, then it is an 'eye'.
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it has been cleaned as we have said in the division, and the cleaning does not help, and you see that the eye is soothed and it is delicate, then you should cover it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	And if it is round and assembled and not long,
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	and it is bloody or of a pale colour or black, then you should avoid incision of it.Quant li sang se pieze par sanz et par veine, il se pieze si fort qu’il ne puet demorer en son leu;
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger to the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	When blood seeps through skin and vein, it seeps so strongly that it cannot stay in its place. Therefore, when you see this happening according to the manner I have described, in terms of its whiteness and length, you should have the patient sit facing the sun, and press his tongue against the instrument which we have mentioned earlier;
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	then insert the needle into the vein, and pull it through, and cut off one of the two strands that I mentioned in the incision of the two testicles.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And you should not cut any more than the surplus which is beyond the natural boundary;
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	because if you cut more, it harms the voice and speech;
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and after the incision, proceed as we have said in the incision of the two testicles, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patient has fear due to covering, then you should use the cautery of the sense of fear.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	The manner of the cautery is for acute fever.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And the patient should put his head down into the healthy person's armpit, and then press his tongue against the instrument that we mentioned in the chapter on cautery, and spit it out with living hot saliva, neither too thick nor too clear;
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and use this instrument, of which there is a description below:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And it has a hair or thread on which to place the medicine, like the hairs of a spoon, and you place the instrument with all the medicine on the eye;
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	and the patient lies on his side so that saliva and mucus flow from his mouth due to the medicine, so that it does not go down into his throat and lungs;
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	then hold your hand over the medicine and press it onto the eye for about half an hour, until you see it swelling and the stinging of the medicine subsides;
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	and if you see that [the medicine] is drying out, take cotton and wrap it around any instrument, moisten the cotton in the medicine, and insert the instrument completely into the cotton onto the eye;
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	and do this often until the cautery is complete, then let it dry and fall off after 4 or 5 days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you need to renew the fire cautery, then renew it, and after the cautery wipe around the eye with cotton dipped in butter, and cleanse what is around the medicine.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let there be washing with cold water, and let there be gargling until it heals.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is safer than incision or cauterization.
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation in this manner, take calendula and hyssop and oregano and rue and chamomile and wormwood and similar herbs, and mix them all or some of them in a pot, and add garlic, and let it boil.
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	And let the pot be well glazed with strong clay, and place the pot over the heat source in this way:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And let it be of silver or bronze, and let one of the patient's eyes be closed with a cloth over their mouth so that the vapors rise to the eye through the nostril until the eye is numbed.
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	afterwards he often repeats it, until the vein dries up, and be careful not to do this at the beginning of the occurrence of a hot abscess, because many things happen;
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	and do not do this until the end of the hot abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not available, take a needle and put an egg yolk inside the tip, so that the mouth on the patient is not too hot;
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	because the egg yolk does not let the steam harm the mouth, and it is a healthy remedy together.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times there is a bone or spine of a fish or something else stuck in the throat;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	so you should pull out what you can see, and press the tongue against the instrument in the sun until you see the object move;
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	and what does not come out and is stuck in the throat, you should make the patient vomit so that the meat is cooked in the stomach;
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	by chance if the thing turns out to be bad through vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	or the patient swallows a piece of sponge, or a piece of turnip, or a lettuce root, or a piece of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and tie the thread to the sponge and then swallow it;
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when it reaches the spot, it will stick there, and then you can pull it out;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it doesn't come out as we have said, then take the instrument of salt according to this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instrument be curved at the tip so that it can enter the throat more easily, and have the tip raised up high;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	and be careful not to touch the epiglottis, or he will choke, nor push anything into the bones inside;
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	and it is better that the patient spits out the instrument when he vomits, so that the thing comes out;
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	if the bowels move downward, or he draws them outward with all his strength, until they are drawn out.
de la sansue de la gorge	of the blood of the throat
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	Sometimes the blood is let, as I have said in the previous chapter, by the use of medicines.
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	And if that does not help, then look into the throat of the patient in the sunlight, and press his tongue with the instrument I told you about.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see the blood, draw it out with a small hook, or with fine tweezers that are fit for this purpose.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if this does not work, take a curved cane, and put it into the throat of the sick person, then put on the curve of the cane hot iron, and do this often.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if the patient has a fever all day long.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	Then take some cold water in a glass, open the mouth, and pour it in without swallowing it, moving it around with his hand frequently;
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	and as soon as the blood feels the water, let it flow out.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	And if it does not flow out as we have said, then smoke the patient with assafetida, using the instrument I described in the section on smoking the throat;
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	do this many times, for it will come out without hurting him.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the way of fuming is that you put charcoal in a pot, and the bottom is covered with a perforated lid, and through that hole the pipe is inserted.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	Then you pour in the smoke, and the patient puts the mouth of the tube in his mouth, closing it so that no smoke escapes, but goes right into the blood.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	And now the blood will flow down, and if it does not, resume the fuming repeatedly.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	And let the patient suffer thirst, and eat salty things, and do not drink water;
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	and then it will be necessary that she go out by this treatment.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the form of the instrument used to draw blood is, when one can see it, like curved tweezers that are bent in order to enter the throat;
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	and has the appearance of a sow's mouth, and it has the roughness of limy earth, so that whomever it bites, it cannot let go;
et vez ci la forme:	and here is the form:
li chapistres des apostemes	the chapter on abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	Mouths that resemble abscesses are, according to what the memory comes later from one and another in this book, and they differ in penetration and size;
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	and there are two ways this happens, either through its own appearance or because of moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second way is for the places where they are in the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	For the abscesses of the head are different from those of the foundations, and the abscesses of fleshy places are different from those that come in joints, and each has its own judgment in the work.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if an abscess should not be punctured until the pus is mature according to its completion;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	and some should be punctured when they are crusty and won't die according to their completion, like abscesses near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	Because when abscesses come from these joints, and one lets them be as long as they are swollen around the edge, perhaps the ligaments and nerves of the joint are corrupted, by which that is caused to contract in that member.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	When the abscess is near the main limb, and you delay the puncturing until it is mature, it will harm the main limb;
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	or if it's near the fundament, it should be punctured as soon as it's mature;
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	and you should not puncture a crusty abscess without digestion being complete, except for one near the fundament, or it may burst inside and cause a fistula;
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	and cannot heal for a long time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And you should know the time of piercing the abscess which is dead, according to its development, and that is when the pain has subsided, and the departure of the fever, and the lessening of the pain and redness, and the softening and hardening of the head of the abscess, and the other signs;
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	and you should make the piercing where the abscess is most dependent, and where it appears soft;
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	and the piercing should be made where it is longest in the body; and if the abscess is in the hands or feet, or in joints, and near nerves and arteries, and in all places where there are no folds.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In those who are bent, according to the affected member.Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when an abscess is in a fleshy place, it is better to leave the puncture until it is confirmed by completed digestion, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce it first, the body will be filled with venom from it, and it is full of filth;
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	and by chance harden the lips and his depths.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And for any abscess that is punctured according to the width of the body, according to what the member needs.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And you must treat with small abscesses, small holes;
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	and in large abscesses, large holes, and many slits according to the appearance of the size of the abscess;
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	and if it has such abscesses where one must cut into the brain, and cover;
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	when it has become as thin as a cloth, and is dead, then one must do as one does with blisters:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	and if there are such that split into three angles, and if there are any that one covers as the pouch of a myrtle berry, just like abscesses of the fingernails;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	and if there are any where one makes a round incision, and other incisions and similar covers.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those that have no head, like a superficial blister, you must pierce fully;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	and when the abscess is large, and he has a great swelling, and you pierce it, do not draw out all of the pus in that hour but only a part.
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	then pack the abscess until the next day, then draw out something again.
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	do this many times from great to greater, until all of the pus has come out.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	especially if the patient is weak in strength, or a woman carrying child, or a small child, or an old and feeble man.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For the pus may sometimes spurt out with the opening of the boil, and the patient might die from it, and you would not realize it.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Therefore, be very cautious when performing this chapter, and when you have pierced the abscess, wash the wound, and see if the wound of the abscess is small;
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	and if it is a clean cut, then apply bandages of linen or old cotton;
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	and if it is a large abscess with many openings, then you must put in each opening a tent so that they come one against the other;
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	and if you have cut into the abscess a part of the skin, and you have seared it all around, then you must fill it with old cotton or linen rags without moisture, and let it lie until the third day;
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then plaster it, and treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if blood flow occurs due to your work, administer cold water and vinegar, and moisten the cloth, and place it over the flowing area many times.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the flow of blood persists, and they administer management and treatment, and the powders that I have described in this book in earlier chapters, and if it is during the winter, and the location of the abscesses is very sensitive, then you should apply hot wine-and-oil-soaked tents and cloths;
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	and if it is in the summer, and the location is fleshy, then you should apply moist cloths soaked in water and oil, or cool wine and oil, for up to a third of a day, as we have said;
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then loosen the abscess, wash it, and treat it as needed until it heals.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	And it is necessary to understand generally in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	I have told you how one should go about treating abscesses, and now see the chapter.
des soros	of sores
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	From the head come small abscesses, and they are caused by us being in fabrics, like the goiter on a goose's neck, and there are many variations of them.Et si li chief est hote, et li leus ou li aposteme est hote, si covient que tu mettes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue fraiche, jusc’au tier jor; puis deslie l’aposteme, essue li leus, et cure-le si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are some that are fatty and others that contain pus and moisture;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	and some are hard and stony in texture, and there is no doubt if the artery does not cause issues.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the work of the abdomen is that you must examine all instruments called "endoscopies", from which the form comes later, what it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if it contains moisture, they will cut it from above.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture has been drained, one should scrape it without leaving anything behind that contains the moisture, because it will return if you leave anything behind.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	Then plunge cotton in Egyptian ointment, if it is present;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	if not, in water and salt, and apply it to the wound and leave it until the next day;
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	and those who are detained at night.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And then resume the cotton, as before, on the second and third days, until you are sure that it does not stay overnight;
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal the wound with an appropriate ointment, until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if the abscess contains pus, then open it according to this method, from the length;
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	and cut your fingernails, and scrape off all the scabs, and put all your ointment to draw out pus from under the skin where it lies;
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	and if the artery pulsates inwards, then do what I told you after this.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And also treat an abscess if it is stone-like, and cut and treat it as I have told you.Si li artere clent, si la traie fuer l’aposteme sus la cotte, tant que li sang ne s’en poie; et si le sang est gras, si met sel et vinyer, et remue li cot ains qu’il s’escanse, et distrai li sang; et se li sang ne s’escante pas, si traie li cot ou il gist sus l’aposteme, tant qu’il s’escanse par le siel de li cotte.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And the incision on the pus-filled, moist abscess is lighter, because there is less blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if any of these abscesses on the head do not contain pus, and they were the abscesses that I described on the head of an old woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and I found the abscess just like a hard stone, rough and white, and could not be broken;
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if one had done it, they would have hurt themselves as much as with a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	For other abscesses coming from the head, especially those that come to the heads of children and to the roots of the ears, the opening should be in the highest and most dependent place so that the pus can flow out.
et les cure si com il covient.	and treat them as they should be.
des scrophules	of scrofula
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Many times abscesses occur in the neck, and under the armpits, and in the groin, and sometimes they come elsewhere in the body, and they are large, and some are connected with each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each scrofula is properly within its coat, like the nodos and the abscess of the head, as we have said;
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	and there are many similarities among these scrofulas.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are some that contain moisture, and there are some that do not obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	In that one therefore which you see of good disposition to touch, and is similar in color to the body, and has no noise in any part and is not cold to the nerves of the neck or to the artery or the channel, and is not deep;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	you should cut it from above, and scrape each part, and the two lips of the heart are hooked, if you have need, as we have said in abscesses of the head;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	and draw it little by little, and be sure that you do not cut the nerve or the vein, nor the artery or the tendons, that the hand does not escape, and do not look too far ahead, lest you cut what you should not.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut the vein or artery, and it will not let you work, put into the wound vitriol powder, or some powders that stem blood flow, and close the wound.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	and leave it until the abscesses are soothed and the wound softens and begins to heal.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the bleeding has stopped, return to your work until you complete it.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then examine with your finger if there are any small scrofulous bumps left, and cut them out and clean the wound.Et si li sans revien, si prends une fiaunce eune espine de rose, ou un peigne, et la mete en la voinne, qu’
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if there is in the root of the scrofula a large vein, you should not cut that scrofula at its root, but ligature it with a strong double thread, and let it fall without harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then dress the wound with old cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment, then cure it.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you cut around the entire scrofula, then you should bring together the two lips of the wound and sew them up now, since there is no longer any surplus due to the size of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	you should proceed to cut around the root of it and pull it out, then sew it up as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	Those scrofulae which have an abundance of pus, pierce there where the pus flows out;
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	and pierce it thus as previously mentioned, so that the pus may flow out; then apply tenting with ointment and similar things, so that it corrupts what remains of the corruption;
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and when the wound is clean, then cure it with ointment mixed with chalk, until it is healed.
de squinance	of scrofula
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The ancients spoke of the cutting of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	but I have never seen it done in our land, and it is written in their books.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those with squint, the fold of the throat called the "epiglottis" should be cut.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	and one does not make an incision through it, because all the veins and the portal of the disease are in those who have a hot abscess in the mouth, or in the throat or in the armpits.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the disease is in the channel of the windpipe, it is necessary to cover the epiglottis to avoid the danger that comes from strangulation.Si li maladie est en la gorge, il covient que tu fendures la gorge et li pormon dou costé, car il ne peut aler si non.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	Therefore, when we want to cut the epiglottis, we should cut it under the two circles or four, a small slit across, between the two circles, or according to the amount of the slit in the soft palate; not in the cartilage.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	and those places where it is suitable to cut the epiglottis so that there is no cartilage, and the vessels are long from there.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the teacher is fearful, then he must stretch the skin of the throat to the very edge, then cut the skin until he reaches the cartilage;
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	and avoid the blood vessels if you see anything, and then cover the wound, as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	and it is demonstrated through the section of the throat where the jugular vein emerges from the broken place, and by the deficiency in voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	and leave the wound open a little.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the hour has passed that we doubt of strangulation, bring together the two lips of the wound in the neck and close it all firmly without the cartilage.
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then administer remedies that promote the formation of flesh, until it is healed.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasim says one should not do this until the throat is completely swollen, and the patient judged dead, and the lack of breath evident.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Then cover the epiglottis so that the patient cannot choke and can breathe through the wound, and thus is protected from death.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	And so the ancients commanded that the wound be left open until the evil of the disease had passed and it is passed in three or four days. And then they commanded to sew up the wound and to treat it, until it was healed.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	and I will tell you what I saw.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I saw a lady take a knife and stab herself in the throat, cutting some of the windpipe;
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	and I was called to heal her, and found her as good as dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I uncovered the wound and found that blood had issued from it, and I judged that she had not coughed up any blood or vomited anything other than through her throat, and the blood was coming out through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurried, and sewed up the wound, and healed her so that she recovered;
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	and the lady had no mark left but a scar on her throat, and returned afterward to her senses;
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	therefore I say that one should have no fear in cutting the epiglottis.
de la grosse gorge	of the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	This kind of abscess is called a "gorge hernia", and it is a large abscess the color of yew wood, and occurs often in women;
et est selonc II manieres:	and there are two kinds:
naturez, et accidens;	natural and accidental;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	the natural kind has no opening.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	And the accidents occur in two ways, one of which is similar to a cyst, and the other way is like an abscess that comes from an artery.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	and there is fear, and one should not operate by force except in the case of a small one, and test and probe at all the orifices:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	if you find it as hard as a cyst, and it cannot be opened by any means, then cut it, as one cuts a cyst, and treat it throughout its entire coat, if there is no pus;
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	and examine it thoroughly, and treat it as it should be, until it is completely healed.
des nous	of us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	There are many types of cysts, all of which I will describe their similarities:
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	and now I will explain the difference between a cyst and an abscess.A cyst is a hard lump that does not open easily, while an issue is soft and can be opened with a needle.The
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that a discharge is heat and feverishness while the ebullition passes, and the swelling is completed.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	therefore, rest the fever and the heat.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	With the nut there is no heat or fever or pain, and it contains a pus-filled sac that is colored according to the body's color, and begins like a jaw, and becomes swollen;
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	and they are according to two appearances: some are dry and others moist, and many colors exist as I have said in the division.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	It is necessary, when you come to the treatment of the pustule, that you examine and inquire into it first with all the instruments called "entromissoires", according to what its form will allow, as described in the chapter that follows.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	And the manner of inquiry for abscesses on the head is that you press in the moistest place that you find in the abscess and move your fingers slowly little by little until you know that the instrument has pierced the core, then according to the size of the abscess.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	Then pull out the instrument and take care in what goes out.Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes qui sont selonc la chair, ou le corps si soit en grand dolor, est qu’on
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	If the moisture runs short, no matter what color it is, treat it as I have said for other abscesses.
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	And if no moisture comes out after the incision, know that it is fatty, so do it in a cross pattern and pick it up with tweezers and lightly scrape each side, and guard the skin where it lies, so that you draw it healthy with the nail.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	And if you cannot draw it healthy, then draw it in pieces so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	For if anything remains, it will return to the body many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if a little remains, and the pain troubles you, then employ some corrosive powders on the wound, and constrict the wound, and put warm poultices on it, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	and if it is large, then cut the two lips of the wound, and clean out that which is rotten flesh.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	and if the pulsing vein is against you or any other, then hasten and apply ground glass, and leave it for two or three days, until the wound suppurates and the bleeding subsides.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	then return to covering that which has been left bare.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	Behold the forms of the intruding instruments, and there are three types:
