grans et moien et petit;	large, medium, and small;and se li estrumen n’a pas la figure en
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	 instrument is not shaped in , and there are three parts which are called "albaret", and one which is called "breb", and there are three types:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	large, medium, and small, to encircle the abscesses of fistulas;
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	are also like the needles used to sew sorcerers, and are made of copper, iron, or silver; those that are yellow in color are more effective, and are best tested with black pitch to surround the curves of a fistula.
et sont de III manieres:	There are three types:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	large, medium, and small, depending on the size of the opening.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of the hooks are very similar, as you can see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	large, medium, and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	and there are hooks with two curves in three ways also;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	and there are hooks with three curves, and they are also of three types;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	and there are hooks with two curves, and hooks with one curve only, and they are of three types;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	and all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The heads of these tools are sharp, and some only cut one side, which they use to shave the skin, so that they do not cut the vein or nerve.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	and for these probes are handles wrapped in cloth so that the patient does not injure themselves when opening abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	There are three types of them:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	large, small, and medium, as you can see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	and they are only used in fleshy places, like legs, arms, breasts, and armpits, and similar places.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	and sometimes a small tool is made, resembling a pair of tweezers, according to this form, with which blood is stopped.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and sometimes it is placed in the place that heals by opening veins and arteries, and sometimes they are bound according to this large form;
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Sometimes the breasts of some men become swollen when they become corrupted, so that they resemble women's breasts.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	and remain unsightly and swollen; and if anyone wishes to cure them, then one must cauterize according to the form of this line .b. up to .g.:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	then scorch the fat, and fill the wound with ointment, then close the two lips of the wound by sewing, and let it heal.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	and if the breast sags downward, and becomes soft because of its size, as happens to women, then they should make two slits above, like two similar incisions;
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	one of which is attached to the other at the end of one and the other, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from this line .b. up to line .g.;et tant com il y ad de graisse, escorche la; si qu’ele soit sanee, et le mamele reposit en son leu;
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then scald the skin between the two lips, and remove the fat, and apply what we have said about stitches and powders, and what is necessary for the treatment, until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	And if it is not healed, or the incision is not fully made, because the patient does not want to rest, or due to blood flow, you should fill the wound with moist cotton in a corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	Let it sit until it absorbs the remainder of the fat, then clean it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	of abscesses of the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses which come under the armpits are types of hard scrofula where there are nodules, and some contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those who contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from line .b. to line .g.:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the bowels which are in the abscess have been emptied, employ the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day; then remove all the cotton and treat it with appropriate ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess is of the appearance of scrofula, they should proceed as we have said in slits for scrofula; and if the wound becomes swollen, they should apply cauterization as we have said previously.Et se li apostemes est desoz le col ou desoz les asseles, si covient que il soit fendu a la radice selonc la ligne m. jusc’a la ligne .g., car en cest lieu il conviens que il soit fenduz selonc la ligne de la nature.
de la routure de l’artere	on the rot of an artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When an artery is cut and the skin above is sewn together, it often leads to abscesses, and likewise, the vein becomes swollen and abscessed.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	And if one knows this is due to an artery, the abscesses are long and deep.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your fingers, you will feel the dislocation;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is in the vein, there is a visible swelling;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to cover this abscess, especially when it is under the armpit and in the groin and neck and many other places, for it is large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	Therefore, one should avoid cauterizing with iron, and if it is on the head, then that should also be avoided, and for the one who has inflammation of an artery under the skin, a slit should be made through the skin above it;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then cut through the flesh with a sharp knife, and carefully separate the artery from the veins, until it is exposed;et puis oevre la cure de fer par le chief ou il est desoz.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then cauterize the head where it is under. Then push a needle underneath and pierce through to the other side, and compress the artery with a double thread in two places, according to what I taught you about extracting the two arteries in the temples;et qu’ele soit bien serree, et que les II perces soient bien coperies, si qu’ele ne se pueda desoufrer.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then point the area between the two ligatures of an introducer so that the pus flows out and the abscess is drained.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then administer the treatment that causes bleeding, until the ligature falls off.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat with an ointment suitable for this, until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is due to an incised wound, you should dye your hand with something that you can get from the abscess all over the skin, then pierce it with a needle held in your hand, and thread a double piece of thread through it, so that you can pull it from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then tie the abscess, as I told you, with one of the two parts of the thread on each shoulder;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you fear that the thread might come undone, pierce another needle with the entire thread all through the abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tighten the thread in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	then scrape the abscess until the pus comes out, then scrape the pus from the wound and leave what is attached.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place a wet cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then administer poultices and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	of abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also, as abscesses come in the arteries and veins, they come to the nerves when they are wounded, or from too much work, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often at the shoulders and elbows and in all joints where there are pustules, and it has the colour of the body, and is in various states without pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when one presses it hard, the patient feels pain, and it is not deep in the body but under the skin.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And it moves in no way, neither forward nor backward, down or up, and the one that is in joints should not be cauterized with iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	Perhaps there might be contraction.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And those who are on the head or forehead, use the spatulum.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with tweezers and squeeze it at its base.
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	For a larger one, pierce it with a needle and drain it, then cut it open, remove the pus, and sew up the wound to heal.
des grosses boces pendans	large bumps hanging
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Sometimes it occurs in bellies and nowhere else; this disease is called "fungus" due to its resemblance to a mushroom, with thin roots and thick leaves.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	There are both small and very large ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	I saw a man with two in his belly that looked more like mushrooms than anything else; they had no difference, were white, had thin roots, and moist fluid ran from them.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them open and found one weighing 18 ounces and the other 6 ounces; the procedure for incising is such that you observe if the disease is moist, and the armpit is white, moist, and has thin roots.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	If the lump is large, apply the spatula widely, and have the fire cautery ready in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For often there are excessive bloodlettings when cutting, and if the blood flows too much, then quickly use the cautery.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	And if you see the patient is terrified and fearful of the iron incision, take a well-prepared thread and tie it around the joint as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	Then release it, and keep tying and untieing the thread around the joint without causing pain until the lump is cut through.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	And if the roots are thick, then fearlessly cut through them for the belly, but you can cut through half of it and cauterize it so that it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and be careful not to cut into the yellow part of the skin which is of poor quality and milky in appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an encrusted abscess, and I will come to the treatment of cancer next.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the boil bursts
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of a hernia comes from cauterization of a wound or fissure in a syphilitic ulcer, and it is on the abdomen and in some of the bowels, as happens in other diseases, or from blood flowing from veins or arteries according to what is mentioned above, or from flatulence;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	And if it is from the disease of syphilis and an exit from the bowel, then the color of the abscess is similar to the color of the body, and it is a minor issue without pain, and it opens in various ways.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the protrusion of the intestine, then it is more varied; and when one presses it with their hands, it retreats, and then comes back out, and sometimes it is blocked, and increases significantly at the entrance of the bath and with intense effort.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it's due to moisture, it's a minor issue, and it opens well when you press it with your hand, and it doesn't constrict.Et se li color est plus fonc que la color dou cors, et n’est pas sens dolor, si est legiere chose, et s’il cort de vo
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if the color is darker than the body's color, and there's no pain, then it's a minor issue, and if it's due to blood, then the abscesses open in various ways: large and hard, and they are fixed according to their size.Et se li aposteme cort de voine
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	and if it is due to wind, then it is soft in the touch, and the actions are such that you observe whether the appearance is due to blood from the artery or vein, or wind.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	Then you must let it heal.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, because of the artery and vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestines or bowels, then you must instruct the patient to tighten his abdomen and hold it straight, then sign around the belly;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then command him to lie down soon between your hands, then go around the area you have signed all around the belly; then let half of the abscess rise up above at the great knuckle;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	then tie it tightly with a strong thread or a strong silk cord firmly, and let the pus be completely discharged;
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	then cut through half of the swollen abscess above the tie, and push your index finger in, and feel for the intestines;
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you remove it from the string, then untie it, and stuff the intestine back into the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the bowel, take it at the anus, and cut off the excess;
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	And if the artery makes you dizzy or the vein, then go around it, then return to your work and take two needles, and thread them with strong thread, and pierce through what you have done in a cross that you are making.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then pull the abscess in four places over the needles, and if you see that the needles are pulling out, remove the needles and let it drain until it can no longer, and cut off the dead flesh by itself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	Or you can cut it when it is thin and draining, then clean the wound as needed, and close up the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and draw out the blood or moisture which you find, then cure the place as it should be, and close up the wound.
dou chancre	from sores
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have described in the section on ulcers the various types of ulcer, how to treat them with medicine, and how to avoid using iron in the treatment.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we say that when an ulcer is found in the body, great care must be taken in its treatment, and the ancients say that when ulcers are in places where they can be reached by scraping, as in breasts, armpits, and similar places, they should all be removed when first discovered.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	And when they are large and old, you must not approach them at all, for I have never seen any healed from such.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	None have ever been healed before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the treatment when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is to sometimes draw out the disease with black bile.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then make him vomit if he shows signs of fullness, then loosen the patient's clothes to prepare for the operation;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then wash your hands and face, and the patient's head and body, leaving nothing untouched;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and let the blood flow freely, and squeeze well the area in your hand or with something else, and if the bleeding from the incision of the artery or vein is not stopped by cauterization, then stop it by tying it off;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal another wound until it is healed.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already discussed in the division the various types of dropsy, and how the accumulation of fluid is caused, and the signs of each type, and how it is treated with medicine, and also by iron.
si est eclites soulement;	if it is only swollen:
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one must not touch with iron in these two cases:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	that is to say, tympanitis and hypothermia, for they are deadly;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	therefore when you treat this appearance of dropsy called by doctors 'ectrotus', and the treatment does not help, look to see if the patient is weak, or if they have another illness besides dropsy, such as a fever and stomach pain and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not touch them with iron, for there is doubt;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient very strong, and they have no other illness except dropsy, and they are not too young or too old, then you must do this;
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	let the patient lie down on his back, and press his belly upwards to force out the water to the lowest part of the feet, then take the spatulum and pierce according to this form;
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And cut into two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	at the tip, and yet not so sharp that it can pierce through to the intestines when pushed in, and not cause bleeding;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then examine whether the dropsy is pressing on the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if you should split open under the armpit three fingers' width straight below the armpit;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is due to disease of the liver, then your split should be on the left side of the armpit three fingers' width;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to the spleen, then on the right, and the patient must not lie on the split so that the excess fluids do not flow to that weak spot;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	then pierce all the way through to the instrument, and stop, and lift your hand to the entire spongy area between the skin and the syringe as much as when skinning in an amount equal to a fingernail or so;
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	then pierce the ulcer until the pus comes to the surface, and this is the color of the pus, then draw it out, and insert this instrument of which this is the shape:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it resembles a slender silver rod, and is made of thin copper or light brass, and has at the end below a small hole:
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side there are three holes:
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one on the other;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes make in feathers:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top is the eye, so that when the instrument reaches the pus, it will drain right into the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	drain off half or a third of it, for if you drain more than is proper in that hour, the patient may die from the loss of his life-fluids, or he will faint, or he will approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to the quantity of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the virtue of the disease indicate, and his pulses;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then treat the instrument and retain the water, which is now retained by the clot that blocks the orifice above the cyst, about which I have spoken, piercing it according to this method:
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then recommence with the instrument the next day, if you see the patient suffering from it, and treat a small quantity of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this every day, and beware of following it as long as there is any water left but only a little.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave it with a lot of water, then treat with hot sand or ash, and with much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and drink some wine;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	and treat with astringent medicines until he is healed, and cauterize the stomach and liver and spleen after the extraction of the pus, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the swelling of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born without an opening on their penis, or the opening is small and not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	If necessary, one must pierce it with a very fine instrument according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then put a plug of cotton in the urethra and tie it and leave it for 3 to 4 days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug and let him urinate, then replace the plug.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and perhaps this is unnecessary because the urine that comes out does not allow it to stay closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	Those whose passages are narrow, if they are medicated with a plug of wool, as we have said, will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have an opening in their place are constipated, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, so they cannot urinate unless they lift their penis upward.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and cannot ejaculate because the material cannot reach the penis, and this is a serious condition.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the way to do this is for the patient to lie on his back, then cut off the top of the penis and foreskin, as well as some of the shaft, so that the hole is in the middle, as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And beware of bleeding which often occurs, and if it does, then stanch the blood with something that stanches blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Many times this albarth comes on the penis, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh;it has a round shape like a testicle, and sometimes it goes away by itself, and sometimes not.if it happens in a woman's breast
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	And there are both malignant and non-malignant ones;the one that is on the penis, if it is large and
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	you must grab them with tweezers very gently, and cut and clean them all, then place wet cotton in Egyptian ointment on top of them.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with the ointment diafinicon until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, discolored and foul-smelling, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have copped it, and if the wound is on the shaft of the penis, with part inside and part outside, then you must first remove the albata that is inside.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And when it is sutured, treat the part that is outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	Because when you treat it all at once, the skin of the penis is not secured so that it does not pierce, and blackness and corruption come to it in its shaft and scrotum.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is necessary to cut away all that is black and corrupted, then lay on the plaster made of honey and flour from pomegranate peels and nuts, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, apply the lunar cautery as follows:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	Cauteries have two uses together: l’un est pour eschauffer le membre et delivre li sang et la
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, with the flow of blood, and corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is damaged and withdrawn, then you should insert a tube into the penis and the patient should urinate through it.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the foreskin is torn at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, whether due to a wound or an abscess, then you must cut it with instruments until all the skin is removed and the head of the penis is relieved of all parts;

de la circoncision	On circumcision:
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a dislocation of continuity like other wounds.
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Nevertheless, when we do this work of our own free will, and properly to children, it is necessary that we do the best and lightest work for their salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of the circumcision of their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have no more than what we have acquired by experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen most of the masters and surgeons who made circumcision all around, and on adults, and on everyone, a new knife.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	It was the cure because there were two membranes, and by chance one above and the other below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now they heal it, covering it, and there is twice as much pain, and in the purification which is due to the wound of the member is not assured its tip.And the member does not look like what it should be, and the wound has a foul smell.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And in the purification of the nail, perhaps the iron escapes and spoils the work, and many times they grow without needing purification, and I have seen this happen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleaning that is done to the foreskin all over the thread I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly above as below.Or li fuit li doler qui tailla l’ungle, si doit il le tailler par fin et non pas par costé, car par fin il ne se peult mander; si doit il estre tailli par costé, et il faut qu’il soit tailli tant qu’il eschieve la chair.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, you cut equally throughout its entire length.
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but the thread must be well-tied around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	and the method of the first operation is such that you cause the child to think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around his penis, and then let him urinate in every way that he can;

Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the force for purification is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two shoulders should be thin and sharp, and the shoulders as wide as the arm equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the error of purification is when the heart inside moves during the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	therefore you must stretch it with your nail so that the skin makes an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and the scalp likewise, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, hold it with tweezers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they persist for three days, and what is under the foreskin is swollen, let it be until the abscess has drained and the skin has healed slightly;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	and cut it as you can, and beware of the part of the foreskin, it will not harm him at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Therefore, cure the place of the sore with powder, as we have said in the treatise on powders, and if they cut the foreskin excessively, and it goes above, it will not harm;et se li apostemes se part a deux ou a III, et sont en la verge, si le laisse tant qu’il soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement, et cure le lieu.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the abscess splits into two or three, and they are on the foreskin, let it be until it is drained and the skin has healed slightly, and cure the place. Cure it therefore as we
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine:
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or frozen blood, or a tumor, or a birth mark, or similar things that we have mentioned in the classification.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not released, and you see that it is retained by a stone which is in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over at the knees:
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And have his feet placed on his back, and extend his belly from above his back, and the patient should hold his breath as hard as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And thus the neck of the bladder is pressed from above to push out the stone, and so the urine flows;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must perform an extraction using an instrument called a "syringe", which is made thus:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and have fine, light silver threads, like a bird's feathers;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and the needle should be about a palm and a half long, with a thin point.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method for urinary problems is to take a doubled thread, tie some wool or cotton at its tip, and insert the tip of the thread into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and twist the excess wool, then fill the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a seat, and anoint the bladder and penis with moist oil and olive oil and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the body;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then fill the syringe until the bladder, and feel the patient come to the empty place, and it is not done according to this order because the person who guides where she goes is wrong.

et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and use the syringe again until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scabs or blood comes into the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see it distilling with water and medicine, then do all the instrument that is called "clepsydra", and that is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you can see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the hair-like channels through which the medicinal cort should pass so that it blocks the penis without addition, and one can draw out moisture and push in when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicines enter the bladder, put the tip of the syringe into the moisture, and draw while pushing the plunger in.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	if you will draw out the moisture from the chest, and then strongly bind it up again;

et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle enema with which one enemas the bladder:
si est ci:	if it is here:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or copper, and the head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and below has the breast or the intestines;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture in it which you want to use for the enema, then tie it between the two breasts shaped like a ball, and heat the pouch over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the head of the enema into the penis, then squeeze your hand on the bladder gently until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment, make a circle out of it, and pierce it all around evenly;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then thread a strong wire through these holes, then assemble the circle as one assembles a jug, and put inside whatever you wish of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, pressing by hand until the moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already said in the division of the stones, and their extraction together with remedies;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have said the difference between a stone lodged in the urethra, and all the signs, and in what kind of stone one should operate with cutting;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the water jumps from the bladder like water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and it opens the urethra, and hurts the patient's penis, and he pees many times, and then it blocks up;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and in many of these cases the foundations (kidneys?) are affected;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the cure is easy for children until they are four years old, but it is severe in the elderly, and it falls in between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with an enema to draw out all the feces that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	Because it sometimes clogs up when seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, lift him up and shake him from side to side, so that the stone descends into the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from above;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have him sit between your hands, his hands beneath his thighs so that his bladder is completely slanting downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then feel and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not come out with just the touch, then moisten your index finger of your left hand with oil, if the patient is an adult, or your middle finger if the patient is young;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into his anus, and feel for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, push it towards the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press on your finger, and push the stone to where you want to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and to extend the testicles upwards with his right hand, and with his left hand to pull back the skin beneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then he cuts the wart, and the spatomyle [i.e., spatulum] cuts it, from which this is the shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	and they cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the navel;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and it is straight on the stone, and both are on the anus, and the incision is diagonal so that it is wide at the top and narrow at the bottom, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure on the anus, the two testicles jump out without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there is such a stone with angles and edges;
si est griés a issir;	if it grinds to come out;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and if there is one underneath, similar to a grape, and round, from which the passage is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	To these therefore where there are angles and edges, make the incision larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not come out, then you must grip it with tongs which are like a file at the tip, to extract the stone so that it does not slip away;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you might push under the instrument a thin, curved hook;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot catch it in that way, then widen the hole and if the blood is oozing, stanch it with vitriol;

Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, then it must be sutured, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things can happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies or the urine comes out again through the hole where the skin cannot heal;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but nevertheless try to draw it out with tweezers, until you have pulled it out piece by piece.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And when you have finished your work, then apply the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and bind it tightly, and put on top a damp cloth wet in oil and wine, or in oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then reseat the dislocation on his neck, and don't loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the site well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it heals.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses and scorched wounds come in the wound, and congealed blood in the bladder, and the urine is retained because of this, known to be in such a way that it comes out with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	then pour boiling water into the wound, and draw out this blood, for if it remains, then the bladder will be damaged and burst.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then raise the wound with vinegar, garlic and salt, and aid him in every way you know until he is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that during all the hours you treat him, you bind his two thighs together and apply remedies to the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	If the stone is small, and it is lodged in the ureter, and pierced through, and the urine cannot pass through;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	if after performing what I have described, you cut him many times, then you are excused from cutting any further by this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take a piece of iron according to this shape and let it be pointed at three angles and fixed in a brand:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis under the stone so that it cannot move back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	then push the rod gently into the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and twist the rod in your hand inside the stone a little at a time until you pierce the stone from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	then immediately the urine will come; press your hand against what is retained of the stone that is within the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it is broken at once and flies out with the urine, then the patient is healed.
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that divides it, then tie a string under the stone and another above it, then make an incision in the penis between the two strings, then pull it out, and untie the string, and cleanse the congealed blood that is in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stone
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Sometimes stones can get lodged in women's urethras, and if this happens, the treatment is difficult due to three factors:First, it is difficult to find the stone because of the narrowness of the passage; second, it is hard to extract without breaking it; and third, it is challenging to cure the resulting wound.Or qu’il n’i aie pas de sang con
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one possibility is that the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second is that one cannot find a well-known woman who reveals herself to suitors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third possibility is that one cannot find a well-known woman skilled in this art of handiwork;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth possibility is that the woman's stone is deeper than the man's, so one must make a deeper incision, and there is great danger in it. And if necessity demands it, you should take a skilled midwife, and with difficulty she will find out about it, and if you cannot find such a midwife, do not desire a chaste one;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present her with a wise old woman who is experienced in the lives of women, or a woman who knows a part of the art, and instruct her to do what you instruct her about the examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look very carefully to see if the woman is a virgin;
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then he must push his finger into her vagina and feel for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, then she should hold it under her finger, and he instructs her to push her finger into the wound and press her left hand firmly against her bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, then she must move the stone from the entrance of the bladder all the way down to the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	then she should push on the stone in the root of the thigh towards the middle of the vagina, where it is most sensitive; and feel for the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and not move her finger above or below the stone, but let the incision be small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then widen the incision if you feel the stone is sharp, cutting the wound so that the stone can come out; and know that there are many types of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	this is to say, small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and which have hairs.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	if you know their appearances in order to understand where they come from.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood flows, put powdered vitriol in place, and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your task, until the stone is out, and have ready the instruments I told you about for extracting stones, with men to assist you in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if the blood flows and it is an artery that is cut, put powder on the spot and hold it with bandages and dressings, and do not release it again, but leave the stone and do not try to pull it out, or the patient may die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the pulse has returned to normal, return to your work until the stone is out.
de hernie carnouse	of carnous hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Red water is nothing other than an assemblage of moisture or white albumen, which is found under the shell of eggs.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and is called "syfac", and sometimes it is properly in the web of the egg, if one thinks that it is another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and this is the skin of the scrotum between the white sac that we have described;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this does not happen often.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the cause of this disease is weakness which comes to the testicles, and that matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it is a declining yellow color, or it is red, or black, or watery white, and there are more variations;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this condition; for if it is in the white sac that we have described, then it is a reasonable abscess, a long poultice as large as an egg, and it does not open the scrotum, for there is moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if it has moisture in the web itself, then it is an abscess with a part of the egg, and for this reason one thinks that it is another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white sac, he feels good;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all over the area, because the shape is in front.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, then, what comes after the intrusion, judge what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, it is necessary that the patient be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then lie on his back on something slightly raised and put a lot of blankets under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then sit on his left, and instruct the assistant to sit on his right, and extend the testicle to one of the two sides of the heart;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the lit spatulum and cut the skin of the testicles between them from the long end to the scrotum, and make the incision straight while cutting the skin of the testicles up to the white sac, and carefully remove the skin according to your strength;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	then pierce the abscess with a sharp knife to a large opening, and draw out all the pus, then put your fingers in, and press the abscess upwards.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the core of the bones, but only the abscess.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	cut it all around or in parts very carefully, and make sure to cut deeply, for if you do not cut deeply, the pus will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the egg white comes out during your work, then reset it in its place once you have finished working on the abscess.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then bring together the two lips of the bone with one stitch, then treat it as you would any other wound until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find that the egg is rotten due to another disease, then you should ligature the veins that are suspended, fearing a flow of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut off the testicle at its attachment, and remove the testicle itself, and treat it as we have described.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if the fluid has gathered into two parts together, know that these are two hernia;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	then cut off the other part in the same way as you did the first, then wash away the blood, and put soft lamb's wool soaked in rose oil into the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put another piece of lamb's wool soaked in wine and oil over the testicles, then place double linen over it, and tie it up with the string following this pattern.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two pieces of linen and stuff them with lamb's wool following this pattern, and sew them together at the crotch of the breeches, so that one piece goes over the buttock to the back, and the other over the groin.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two chiefs above the two angles, and the entire restraint must be gathered in the loop of the bandage.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this ramice of cautery is medicated in place of the iron knife; and you must grip the subtle cautery knife, and cut the skin of the testicles, and it should be heated as we have said so that the white pus contained in the water is revealed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	if one takes the cautery according to this form and pierces that testicle with it, and scorches it with this subtle hot cautery;
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And scrape it in every way you can, until you draw it all out.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and beware that the fire does not touch the testicle;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and while being mindful of bloodletting, and changes in the testicles;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if nothing makes it worse, such as an abscess, or bloodletting, or anything else, then treat what makes it worse, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and unwilling to undergo this procedure due to its horrifying nature, then perform incision as I have told you, and when you are certain from the signs we have discussed that the water has been expelled, have the patient sit up on a high seat.
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	Then pierce the abscess at its base all the way to the underlying tissue, and place the incision at the longest part of the body.et adonques remens li cors a son leu; et s’il s’estrange ou se retuit, si tuit li corps en sa guize, ou
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And then return the body to its proper alignment; and if it becomes dislocated or twisted, then adjust the entire body in its natural position, and broaden the incisions so that
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton over the wound, dress it, and leave it to drain the remaining fluid, then treat the wound until it is healed.et si la mort vienne dedenz, il ne te doit moudre, por ce qu’il a paor et doute de la mort;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white membrane does not let water out of the mouth of the wound, then you should apply a tube or instrument to draw out the water as with dropsical patients, whose form is described above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and dilate the wound, and know that the water will return, and is collected after six months or so around it, and when it is collected as before, then the disease will run its course.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the cutting of this vein there is fear in many dispositions, because of which I think it better to leave it alone;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the treatment and the appearance of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses come from the body, especially in the groin;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this is by far the most common case.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is known to be caused by excessive bitterness and bile, which is spread to the groin, or from a blow;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and does not hurt, and is a serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes an abscess is grey and purulent, with a pus-like appearance, and at other times it comes from a vein, or inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from a vein, it is recognized by the warm feeling of the abscess when pressed with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	That which comes from inflammation of a vein is recognized by its appearance when pressed with the fingers, and one can safely lance it according to these signs, and in the same way for the others;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and it is necessary to cut the top of the egg-white, then the yolk will come out on its own, and the membrane will be released from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the eye is sore from these new ointments, then you should wash the eye, and the lid.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if there is an ulcer in the eyelid, or on what is inside the eyelids, then you should free all that tissue and wash it thoroughly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the yolk is at the back end, then you must open it all and remove the yolk as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then dress the wound with soft lambs' wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to the bud of a branch, with the softening of the testicles, and it causes great pain when the patient urinates.
