et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment for this disease is just as fearful as that one above, and yet we shall tell you about it according to how the ancients did it.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You should make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then squeeze the testicles with your fingers towards your body at the part where they are attached to the root of the penis, and tie them tightly, pulling them upwards.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then cut the skin with a sharp knife across the vessels, so that they are uncovered, and then scorch on each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries which are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then he inserts a needle with a doubled thread, and ties it at the first place where the vis came out, and ties it directly to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then he cuts them in the middle, following the length of the body, and draws out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then he treats the wound as in the others, so that no blood vessel that nourishes one of the testicles is cut;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	because no harm comes from it, and if blood comes from all the vessels, then one must draw out the testicles from all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the vein does not lose its nourishment because of the incision of the vessels, and dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rot of the sinus
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The cause of this disease is due to the incision that comes from the syphilitic sore, or the swelling on the abdomen in the region of the intestines, causing them to descend from this passage to one of the orifices.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this passage is either from the syphilitic sore or from the swelling; and these two types arise from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	either from a blow, or jumping, or screaming, or lifting a heavy object, and from similar activities;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs that it is from the swelling of the syphilitic sore are that it happens little by little over a long period of time and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are even throughout, towards the depth, because the syphilitic sore presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs of dislocation of the shoulder blade are that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and there are various abscesses under the skin near the surface, which is due to the exit of the intestines and the body being displaced by the shoulder blade.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the nerves are displaced with the intestines, and it is retained inside, causing great pain to the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments, one should fear, for which it is necessary to avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the way to treat it is to instruct the patient to pull the intestine back into the wound with his hand if he can reach it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then rub his neck between your hands and lift his hips;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then they cut the hair on top, and shave all the hair from the long neck;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then cut the skin around the navel with knives according to what you need to open the wound, and it should be such that the intestines can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape off the skin under the hair on the scrotum, until the white scrotum is exposed all around;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	then insert your index finger into that which is under the scrotum, in that which is between the white scrotum and under the skin of the testicle, and between the second scrotum, and separate that which is behind the testicle, and between the second scrotum;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	then move your right hand to the scrotum, and hold the white scrotum up in your left hand, and lift the testicle with all its skin towards the navel;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to extend the arm upwards, and loosen what is tight behind the elbow;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your fingers if there is any tough, white membrane or intestine wrapped around it, and if you find anything, push it back into the belly below;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with a thick thread made of six threads, and insert it into the back part of the sac, which is behind the skin of the testicles;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the needle has passed through the sac, then grasp the head of the needle with your fingers so that there are four threads hanging;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then tie the threads one above the other in the shape of a cross, and bind the sac, which we said is under the skin of the testicles, with a strong knot made of two parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the head of the needle and threads, and tie it firmly with two parts so that none of the vessels that supply blood to it can enter, lest an abscess forms there;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and apply the cautery according to the first long line of two lines from that, and after these two lines, leave the syphilis which is under the heart of the testicles, the larger one of the two;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then all the other according to the roundness that the egg carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut into the part which is under the skin of the testicles, until the blood runs, and the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply moistened wool in oil, and place it on the wounds, and then apply the cautery that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, out of fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens many times, and leave the cautery until it cuts through it;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it is slow to cut, then use hot water, and apply what we have described until it cuts through;et s’il ne se peut checier per lui, si covient il remestre la piere de selonc la dislocation que nos avons dit.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then cure the wound with another cure, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of carnous hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this chapter I have never seen anyone dare to perform the treatment with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like the thread that is together with the thread, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after the incision above, slightly under.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut it halfway, and cure the abscess of what opens, until the vessels drain;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and cure it as we have said, until it is healed.Et s’ele ne veut chier, tu l’endures par guaiace et par baume, si com
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	And if it does not drain, you endure it with a poultice and ointment, as we have said, and the abscess breaks open, as we have said, and the pus drains out;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and none of the intestines come out, and if any do come out, it is a little, and they heal every hour;Et s’el est si grande qu’ele soit a grant dolur, tu la fendes en deux ou en trois partz, si que li sang ne deffuit point, et l’endures tant que li
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and yet if it remains too long in this condition, the wound or fistula will increase in size as the intestines descend.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens due to the extension of the fistula, which is in the anus, as we have said, because it extends and then becomes soft and swollen and open;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment for this is through cauterization, as we have previously stated;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is cured by iron in the following manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and let the patient lie on his back between your hands, then press down on the area around the wound, according to its size, a palm's width at a time;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then pull out the fistula which is under the skin, then take the reed and place it on the visible area of the fistula;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press it deeply into the belly, then cut the two visible ends of the fistula on top of the reed, cutting them one after the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull out the head of the rope, and do not cover it with anything or stretch the ureter or anything else, as I have made you aware in the treatment of the ramus of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it according to the treatment for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, cleanse and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The syphilis is hidden, and has no appearance in the mouth; and the cautery is effective in this place, and is closer to a cure.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	from the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Often the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men due to the organs within becoming soft, and it is visible;
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and when one wants to treat it, they must make the patient lie on his back, and cut the skin that is soft on top of the skin of the scrotum;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then bring together the two lips with one stitch, and if you see it, sew the excess of the soft skin firmly with three or four stitches;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	then cut between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	from chastity
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is prohibited by our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to discuss it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and is only necessary for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	the first is so that the doctors know how to respond when asked, and know how to treat it;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other is because we often need castration of certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and pigs and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	Therefore I say that castration is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by吸引or by cutting.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	For the one that we do by吸引, we make the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are soft and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then grab them with your hand and hold on until they come off and you no longer feel anything.Et li autr’est selonc la fente que nos faisons sur la chair a la fine de la verge, dont suit l’evacuation de
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the castigation of the waist:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you must tie the beast, and press the hide of its testicles in your left hand, then slap the suspender, and hit each testicle once, when you have well-scorch them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave some pus of the scrotum and the subtle scrotum which is under the testicles;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this type of castigation is better than that which is done by pulling, because with pulling, something might remain in the testicles, causing the beast to desire lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then cure the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	There are two types of hermaphrodites in men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is where between the two testicles appears what looks like a woman's vagina, with hair, and sometimes it urinates in this position.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and has on the little finger as well as a rod and two scrotums.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment of both man and woman is that you cut off the swollen testicles, and treat them like any other wound;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second manner, men from whom the urine jumps through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the testicles
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is a scar formed on the natural part, so much so that it is too ugly to look at;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You should dye the excess of the tentigene with your hand or fingernails, and then scratch it gently;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, lest bleeding occurs, then the cure of one cure until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and at another wound that occurs at the mouth of the wound, and use it, and perhaps it will jump out, and is according to the appearance of a cow, and for this reason they called it "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must cope with it, as we have said about the tendon, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Irregularity occurs when the nature of a woman is not understood, or the opening is small.
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	It can be natural from birth, or it can be an accident caused by illness that arises in it.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	Or it is due to a stricture, or a thin or thick membrane, and it is made deep inside the stomach, or on the sides, or underneath, or wherever it may be.
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	And it affects conception, childbirth, and potentially flowering.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	And the understanding of this is through observing the dance.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the stumps are visible nearby, you can pick them with your fingers or with a stick.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is due to a thin membrane and it is close to the lips, then you should be quick about it, and they will heal thusly:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread out.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then press the lips together until the thin membrane is punctured and the swelling goes down.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it on the area; have the woman lie still each day so that it may not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the sty is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatula like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the wound is from a new birth, then suspend it at the umbilical cord and the navel;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have stanching medicines, such as aconite, dragon's blood, incense, and egg white;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then administer a wide-mouthed jar, so that the wound may not heal;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and in this way for a long time, and then administer a tent made of dry linen;Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is from a new birth, then suspend it at the umbilical cord and the navel; and then perform other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when there is flesh damage, it should be cut according to this manner, unless it is an ingrown abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For in an ingrown abscess that is in the joint, one must not cut.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings in the veins which usually happen without cause, and when they are old they become thrombosed;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have already discussed in the division the similarities of ears, and the signs, and I will now describe those which are curable.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and thrombosed piles, when they are deeply embedded in the rectum, and do not appear to the touch, are not cured by the application of a hot iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those that are at the mouth of the rectum, which one can feel, can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you should put the woman in a cold room, then pull out the hair with tweezers, and apply powder to the roots made from blood-restraining medicines, such as aconite and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, then place her in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if there is bleeding, then have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel and galls, and similar things, and then take barley flour, and boil it with honey and garlic, and make a plaster from it to apply to her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it is staunched, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, then have leeches applied to her back and breasts without bleeding;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take lamb's wool, soak it in plantain juice or dogwood juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has drained, treat the area with ointment until it is healed.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And that which is called "albathir" is red and resembles rough ash; it should be covered as I have said before.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	of abscesses in the anus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses occur in the body, such as ulcers and pus-filled sores, herpes, cysts, and hemorrhoids, as well as hot abscesses, and several other ailments which I have mentioned in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I shall discuss in this treatise the hot abscess that occurs in the bowels, which is not among those that occur in the body:
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you want to know about the treatment of iron, then observe whether the abscess is hard at the beginning of its appearance, and filled with heat and fever, and whether it turns red if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it heal as long as the pain is relieved;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a chair, and have two small chairs on which to lean, and support his back and gather his feet towards the affected leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let his thighs be spread out, and he should place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good rope;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then open the wound towards the right side, and administer the instrument to open the mouth of the wound, from which the form comes afterwards;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you see the instrument administered, you push it in slightly at first to determine the depth of the wound, so that what goes into the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and it does not harm the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instruments are larger, then they must cover the depth of the wound with cloth so that the instrument does not harm them;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and one should place the tip of the instrument on top and grip it tightly.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess has been opened and they have done so by hand, then they must cover it with a bandage around the head or shoulder.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowels are emptied, then one must put into the wound wet tenting soaked in rose oil or in dry green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the tenting over the wound at the bottom of the wound, and put another bandage over the wound and over the clean finger wet with water or with mallows that have been cooked;
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then the wound will be cured after two days of ointment, as long as it is healthy;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes we raise it and cure the wound with a clyster of water and honey, and then of water in which roots of iris and aristolochia have been boiled for a long time;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is depressed into the injury, then you should be careful not to cook with iron, but heal it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary for the midwife to first know the natural shape of childbirth and the signs; when you see the woman push downward and desire to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child will hurry to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is according to nature, and the birth canal is under his head, and the afterbirth with him;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, then you should gently press her belly so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when he descends upon his head, the afterbirth comes with him, and the birth canal is cleansed of its excesses by good cleaning;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and this which comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it sometimes comes on its feet and comes out of the body or the shoulder, and the hands, or it comes over his stomach, or under, and is accidentally turned around his neck, and in other evil shapes;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the doctor to be wise and subtle in these matters, and beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the shapes and how one should help them.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out on top of his head through a natural opening, and the mother gives birth painfully, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a saddle, or have women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and put the doctor's small spatula, of which I will now describe the form, between her lips:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the membrane, and scrape with his nail until the fluid that is within runs out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's abdomen so that the fetus descends, and if it does not descend, then the woman should be given a clyster of fennel with oil of sesamum.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her press and sneeze with this condiment, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Now if the child is born immediately.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands come out, you must then gently push them back in a little bit at a time.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	And if they cannot go back in, place the woman on a seat, and elevate her feet.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	Then lift the seat off the ground, and tighten it around the woman so that she does not slip while standing up.et si le corps ne puet aler par le col, si covient le clysterier de fenugrec et oile de sisament;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	And if the body cannot go through the neck, then she should be given a clyster of fennel and oil of sesamum. And if the hands cannot go in and the child is dead, cut off the fingers at the knuckles as mentioned earlier, extract the child, and reset in the same way.Et si li enfes ne puet aler par le col tant qu’il soit en la mort, et tu n’i poues faire que
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the birth of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes out feet first, it must be turned upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	And then turn it bit by bit until it is straight;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	Then grasp one of the feet and stretch it out bit by bit.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If it jumps up to the crotch, instruct it to grab hold and make it sneeze from that position;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it jumps out, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it doesn't jump out as we have said, then slowly turn it back to its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it is easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come out as we desire, take myrrh, tall oil, gum mastic, and grind them all together in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and apply this ointment to the woman's private parts and make her sit in warm water up to her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is softened underneath, place the myrrh collar underneath her and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a stool, then make her sneeze and constrict her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child will jump now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	the child will emerge onto its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this way, he puts his hands on it little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then he is put to rest on his neck, and his feet hang down, and he lies on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bends his arms little by little, and then he presses his hands on her belly, and takes the cushions from under her, so that she is straightened out below;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, he takes his feet and moves them about, then he moves her belly upwards, then he puts his hands in;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and makes the baby jump little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instructs the woman to press until the child emerges.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the emergence of the child who comes out with one hand hanging down
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	I must devise a way to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be brought back, then have the woman rise and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she cannot walk, then have her lie on the bed and lift her legs straight;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then bring the mouse trap that I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a chair, and then try to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and hold the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and command that she grasps it until it comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the child's exit above its neck, and spread her hands, and turn her face towards her mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	Let the assistant grab her hand, then slowly turn it back and forth, and wiggle it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, place the mouse trap of alatris and oil, as we have said, then command that she moves it slowly back and forth;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, have her sit on a chair, and instruct her to hold herself steady.
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for all the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When all the mucus has come out in this way, catch it with your finger so that the moisture is expelled;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if phlegm rises to her face and throat, catch it with your hand so that it is not retained and the infant dies;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the infant back inside, ensuring that he is placed correctly, and instruct the woman to hold herself steady several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	then she will be cured easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the hernia
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	You should know that twins are born many times, and sometimes three or four are born at once;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange occurrence, it happens often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are strange, and they do not live long if they do;
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know them, that they are multiplied, and are separated by the styptic that divides them, which is bound to the wound.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they emerge as naturally as a tail, just as we said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they emerge quickly, then the cure is as we have said, and the surgeon must be skilled, and do quickly and lightly what he does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and act in such a way that it benefits their health.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the womb one, or two, or three, or four, or five, or six, or seven, or more up to fifteen, and are all formed in the shape of a child according to the measure of the glorious sage, and the surgeon must know all this because sometimes similar things happen;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	and he must act accordingly.
de l’enfant mort	of a dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are curing a woman of a dead child or abdomen, as I said in the division, and no pus comes out, and you are compelled to use your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if you must know whether the woman is of sound mind and has no incident where she fears death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	the woman should be laid on her back, with her head inclined downward and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the midwife should apply the herbal remedy to the perineum, or if necessary, the woman should be tied to the bed to prevent her from giving birth;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils infused with marshmallow root and fenugreek and flax seed, then anoint the midwife's hands with these oils and herbs;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then press gently on the mother's stomach, then push upward where she feels the urge to push, and take care that the child does not descend head-first;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if the child's fingers are stuck in her own orifices or mouth or throat or under the chin or near the ears or on either side of her head, and if the descent is toward the feet, then push or pinch where you feel resistance;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he must hold the needle with his right hand, and place the thread between his left fingers, and wind it around his whole hand lightly, and insert the needle in one of the places we have described, so that it comes to the empty spot;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the shape of the needle:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another needle, or a third if you need it, so that the extractions are equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they are moved equally from one side to another, so that they exit; and the needles are bitten down to hold them in place, as shown in this image:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if some remains, he should smear oil on one of his fingers and insert it into that part, and pull out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if none remains, he should put that needle or another higher up, and do this until it all comes out firmly.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be returned by stretching, then you must wrap it in a cloth, so that it hangs completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then place the cautery on the joint of the palm or the wrist, and you must do the same for the other hand and also the feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of the child is large and it is stretched out in delivery, or if it has an acute head gathered there, you must push the spatulum between your fingers, press the head, and extract the fluid.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Or you can use the instrument called "almidach", from which the shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And likewise, do the same if the child has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	And then pull out the bones with pincers, and if the head pops out and is dislocated by force, it will be split as long as the fluids inside the head exit;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it off piece by piece as you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if he is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce him so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, the pull is light, and the movement towards the mouth of the wound is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if he is constipated in the belly or anus, then you must stretch him with a cloth wrapped around his hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the belly or anus so that the moisture runs out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other members are swollen and the urine does not flow, then he should hold his hand over the wound and pull it up to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then he puts in his finger or two and pulls it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed by a hot abscess that has formed there, one should not work on it, but rather apply moist and greasy substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the minister applies poultices, and soaks it in warm water that softens and moistens.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the hernia is on his side, and you can make it even, then administer what we have said about the living child:
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no power over it, then treat it bit by bit and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, administer what we have said about hot abscesses that come in the belly;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if blood-letting comes about, then it should be put into restraining water and other remedies administered.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly some fetus had been dead, then another was sewn over it, and the other died as well.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came in her armpit, and swelled so much that it opened, and began to discharge profusely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the priest, and I thought for a long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attractive plaster, and an bone came out, and after a few days another one did too.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I probed the wound, and in so doing pricked some bones until the woman was in a better state;Et si li fuert l’os traiet, si le tuit sanz quebrure, et la plaie curat.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And if the bone was pricked, then it should all be done without breaking and the wound healed.And so the woman lived a long time like this, and sometimes she felt a bit of pain in that spot;Et si li fuert l’os traiet
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter only because when the masters find a strange thing, they know to apply a remedy.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the dislocation back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the form of the press, which is described in books:
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and has two turns around the two shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns of the restrictor should be more subtle, made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the tube should be two digits wide and the rim of the trees one and a half palms long;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in between the two limbs there should be two ajustments of this same wood, which are firmly attached to both, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two adjustments are fitted into the mouth of the tube in order to open it when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, which is more subtle and lighter, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the likeness of tongs:
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and has two heads, as you can see, one palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the woman open to all instruments, make her lie on her back with her feet hanging and her legs open, then insert the two instruments together into the wound, and hold the head of the instrument between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the instrument, just as you did with the tongs equally, according to the amount that you see open the mouth of the wound, until the midwife does what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all tipped and have many variations in their appearances;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the midwife has prepared them, then the work is swifter and higher in men due to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not be discouraged by the instrument until you have prepared it, for their needs are not preventable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold in her breath and then make her sneeze from time to time, and squeeze her hands around her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if she jumps through the air, all is well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take the pot and make a cover for it, placing herbs inside that can open the mouth of the wound, such as comfrey, fennel, anise, chamomile, cassia, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or any of them, should be cooked in the pot over fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then place one end of a rod or stick into the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the wound, and hold it there until the vapors enter the wound;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then the secondine suddenly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she still remains after this treatment and does not recover, instruct the midwife to wet her left hand in oil of wormwood or in a poultice of alder buds, then insert it into the birth canal and extract the placenta;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, she should grab and extend it little by little straight, so that the bone does not break upon extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled.
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come out easily.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is tight, we have discussed the cure for sneezing, and the fumigation of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not improve with what we have said, then you must be careful when pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that whoever is at the mouth of the wound, should tie it to the thigh of the woman, then cleanse with the four-part ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will come out and return;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but nevertheless, when it comes out there may be a foul odor in the stomach and head, and it will harm the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Then smoking is necessary for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	one of the ancients has experimented with fumigation of watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one smokes out the woman for the retention of flowers and afterbirth, if it is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass resembling a cane, and the thin end is placed in nature, and the broad ends above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and the fumigation is on the coals, and the lice until they are destroyed, and then start another.
de percier lou fondement	of piercing the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foreskin pierced, but the skin is closed with a subtle slit:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	then one should at the circumcision pierce that slit with her nail, and not cut it with a sharp blade, and guard against touching the foreskin.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put on wet milk with wine and oil, then the ointment cure until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, then put a splint of wood through the wound, and leave it for several days, and remove it when the child wants to walk.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this clotting comes from a wound or abscess suddenly;
si covient coper celui soudement:	Then one must suddenly cover this.
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it is to be cured, as we have said about the vein of the penis.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula in the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from under the buttocks are nodular and grow from beneath the anus, or in the space between the two halves of the anus, and may be single or multiple.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when this nodule is old, it opens, and usually there is moisture that causes white pus or thin fluid, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent.si est en la fesse ou deuz la cosse si a grant dolor sus les testiculos et les cosses, si covient elever celui membre tant com il puet, et si le covient adoucer, si doit adou
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers. Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are sores that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach all the way to the hip joint, and to the bottom of the groin.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows a fistula piercing in the anus, and not piercing at all:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you push your index finger into the anus, and push a thin bronze or iron needle into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it has twisting, then you insert a flexible wire, or horsehair, as far as you can feel the wire or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and it does not cause any evacuation, wind, or pus, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	then you know it is not piercing through;
si te haste dou curer.	if you wish to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula extends to the bladder or the urethra, and the urine leaks out, and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced to the hip joint, then the tented vein will reach that spot.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no tortuousness and the pain is not relieved by it, then it will not be helped by medicine or ointment.s'il n'y a pas de tortuosité et que la douleur ne soit pas soulagée par elle, alors elle ne sera pas aidée par la médecine ou l'onction ;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persisting fistulas there is no cure despite effort and the vain attempts of foolish doctors who interfere.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those that are not persisting and are not old, there is hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and he should raise his legs up to his hips, and have his hips tilted towards his stomach;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then push in a tent of bronze or lead if there is tortuousness, as far as you know the vein goes.puis boute une tente darain ou de plonc si il y a tortuosité  ;
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the pain is felt around the anus, then you must insert your finger, provided that the skin has not been pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and it should be uncovered where you feel between your finger and the flesh, then you will know that it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if it cannot be reached, then it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	They say nonetheless that some can be healed, but that happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is done, one burns the cautery subtly according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and pour it all hot into the fistula, until it comes out through the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that those charred flesh pieces are burned, which resemble an owl feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then the cauterization with moist tents until that swelling goes down, then the application of ointment to bind and heal.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is not done, they cannot be healed otherwise.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if the tent pierces and does not reach the bone which is in the foundation, and there is between your finger and the tent a thick covering of pus or of syrup, and you see the fistula below the covering of the flesh;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If you cut off the beginning of the fistula and fill it up before the tent, and then cauterize it afterward, until it reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	And the tent will be delivered, and it will fall out;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then cut off those false growths that look like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus runs out, and flows between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery joins two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	Here is the translation: This includes scorching of these swollen cars, and oozing of blood and drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of moist tents with butter or crushed substance, until the swelling goes down and the burned cars heal;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound of sudden, painful, hard growths on the body, and the remedies are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way from the anus, and is separated from the body, put your finger in it or plug it up, and ask for help.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you sense a tent, and within it is a thread or string, or the growth, or it is about to pierce through, then there must be no fear or despair, but rather hope and expectation, through the administration of one of three remedies:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it down to the bottom, or if you can, put in tents and treat it as before;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep that you do not cut the lining that holds the foundation, and let the discharge come out through there naturally;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and clean it once it has been cut away from the foundation, or with a tent or another pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then pierce the infected bone in the wound as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then work to heal the wound and to stop the fistula from draining into the abdomen:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is more convenient for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are like this:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is on the side next to the abdomen, take a pointed tent shaped like this:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And thread .ii. threads through it, and push the tent all the way through the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is deep in the margin of the abdomen, then pull out the thread from that hole, so that you can push your finger into the abdomen;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and draw the head with thread, and bring the two heads together, and tighten them against each other, and leave it for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it sometimes, until the threads cut through the flesh between them, and they separate.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then cure the wound so that it heals and scabs over.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not burst, then have it burst in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because it is not appropriate to bandage too tightly and then to treat, as we have said, until it has healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny spatulum used for making a fistula is very sharp on one side, and pointed;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is not, so that one does not cut what one should not cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	There are two types of hemorrhoids:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	or they are inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they ooze blood, and there is one or more of them, and they are found inside and at the top of the anus;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those which are out of joint have little moisture, and still a little water or a little yellow water or a little blood, and they have the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them in the anus is that you instruct the patient to defecate so that the anus opens and the threads appear.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	Take it with tweezers or hold it with your fingernail, then pull it out at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the tweezers cannot hold it because of the moisture, take it with a piece of cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois leather;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	pull them out with your fingers, then cut them, and powder them with some hot powder that is in the place of cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you can cauterize it as mentioned in the chapter on cautery, after treating them with other remedies until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the fundament cannot emerge, then enema the patient with a sharp and asperous enema to wash away what is in the fundament so that it can emerge openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	then the patient should strain, and if the thread comes out from the fundament, then the cure is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should grab them with your nail or tongs and cut them, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed and the incision closed with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	You must administer the suturing in the following manner:Prens li fil de l’asne ou del mazuret, ou del garse, qu’il soit fort et leg
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a strong and thin thread of donkey, mare, or horse hair, twist it tightly, thread it into a needle, then pull the two ends of the thread through the eye of the needle from one side and back out the other, leaving a loop. The thread should be twice as long as the wound is wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tighten the thread tightly, then tie the thread, and pull out the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to stop the flow of blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place a wet cloth soaked in rosemary oil or cerate over the wound, and apply pressure to the wound, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him go until he defecates, and when he has finished, treat the wound with ointments and other remedies until it heals.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the vagina or anus
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is dryness of the bowels in the intestines, and due to the constraints of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If necessary, cut off the nail at the quick, or use a spatulum to remove the loose piece of nail, being careful not to damage the nailbed.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then treat the wound as needed until it is clean and healed.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	If it cannot heal, then re-cut the nail more aggressively than before, until it heals and is smooth.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat until healed.
dou fremit	where it trembles
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A wart is a small growth on the body, which moves deep inside;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes the wart chills, and one feels it as numb, and it comes all over the body, but more on the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And its treatment is to take a feather from a goose or a strong owl, and place that feather on the numbness until the purple circle around the numbness disappears all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand over the entire feather until you cover all around the numbness, and push it deeply, and pull out the numbness from its roots.
