Et si a de ces qui dient qu’il le covient aministrer viandes qui enflent le ventre, por bouter la briseure au defuer.	And if there are those who say that one should administer foods that swell the belly, in order to push the fracture outward.
Nos ne faisons mie ceu, que apostemes chaulz n’i viegne, s’il n’i est venus.	We do not agree that hot poultices should be applied if they have not already been used.
Et s’il i est venus, si le saine.	And if it has come, then heal it.
Et dirent aucun d’ous c’on met ventouses sor le leu, por sucier forment, et c’est semblant a raison;	And some say that one should apply cupping glasses to the area to suck out the bad blood, and that makes sense.
toutevoie, doutance i a que li ventouse n’atraie les superfluitez au leu por la disposition de foiblece.	However, there is a doubt that the cupping glass draws out the excess fluids due to the weakness of the body.Et si le ventouse ne peut etre, metes sor le leu un pons d’espeine, ou d’osier, qu’il fust fort et as pre
Et dirent aucun d’ous c’on doit covrir le leu de lainne moillie en oile chaut, et met on tentes entre les costes por metre igal la lieure entor, puis soit curez de la cure de pleurisin, de viande et de medicine.	And some say that one must cover the affected area with moist woolen cloth soaked in warm oil, and place tenting between the ribs to apply pressure evenly all around, then it is treated with the treatment of pleurisy, meat, and medicine.Et autrui dit que l’on doit covrir li leu de lainne seche et de velle, et mettre oile chaut sus li leu; puis soit curez de la cure d’esguarison, et de medicine.
Et se li malaides sent grant dolor qu’il ne puet soffrir par l’os qui point la toile, et doutance est au malaide, si covient fendre sus lou leu de la coste brisie, et covient mettre desoz I estrument por warder lou syfac;	And if the patient feels great pain that they cannot endure due to the bone pushing against the lining, and there is doubt about the patient, then one should split it open at the site of the broken rib, and one should place an instrument underneath to push out the pleural fluid.
et adonques doit on trenchier l’os, et traire legierement, et puis coudre les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, et le curez d’emplaustres, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then one should cut the bone, and gently pull it out, and then sew up the two lips of the wound if it is large, and treat it with plasters until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient, si met sus drapelz moilliez en oile roset, et met sus lou leu;	And if a hot abscess comes, one should place wet rags soaked in rose oil on top of the site, and
et cure tandis le leu de ceu qu’il covient a aposteme, et soit gisans sovins sus lou costeit ou il doit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	treat the area around where the abscess should be, and let the patient lie carefully on their side where it is, until it is healed.
de la brisure dou col	of the fracture of the neck
Aucune fois vient briseure as os dou col, et poc avient k’il ploie;	Sometimes a fracture occurs in the collarbone, and it pops out;
et ausi a l’espinee dou dos.	and also at the spine of the back.
Et quant ce avient a aucun, et tu vues savoir s’il sera sanez ou non, si pren warde se tu vois ses mains mollifiies et enflees et mortes, et ne les puet movoir ne estendre, et quant tu les poins d’une aguille, si ne lou sent.	And when this happens to someone, and you want to know if he will be healed or not, take note if his hands become soft and swollen and numb, and he cannot move or straighten them, and when you prick him with a needle, he does not feel it.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz em plusors dispositions, et s’il les muet et sent bien quant on les estraint et point, saiches que li jointure de l’os est sauve, et que li malaides iert curez, s’on i met cure.	Know that it is deadly in many cases, and if he becomes mute and can feel nothing when you dislocate and prick him, know that the joint of the bone is safe, and that the illness is cured if treatment is applied.
Et se semblans chose vient a l’espinee dou dos, et tu vues savoir s’il iert sanez ou non, si pren warde se li piez sont amollis, et se li accident i sont qui sont em mains, et sus lou dos saut ventositeit et egestion sens volonteit;	And if similar things come to the spine of the back, and you want to know whether it is healthy or not, take note if the feet are swollen, and if the symptoms are in the limbs, and on the back, wind and defecation without intention;
et quant on l’a sovineit sus son ventre, si saut egestion sens volonteit.	and when he is lying on his stomach, there is defecation without intention.Si li accident i sont qui sont em mains, et s’il a dolour sus son ventre, et sotilité en ses piez, et sotil
Et quant il est sovinez sus son dos et il vuet asseller, si ne puet.	And when he is lying on his back and wants to sit up, he cannot.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz:	If the symptoms are in the limbs, and he has pain in his stomach, and weakness in his feet, and weakness
si ne laboreir mie en sa cure.	if he does not labor in his healing.S’il sotile en ses piez et sotilité en son ventre
Et se cist accident ne li vienent, si est li chose plus legiere.	And if this does not happen to him, then the case is lighter.
Et li cure si est que tu rewardes s’il i a aposteme chaut, si met sus l’espinee oile roset ou oile de moieuf d’uef, tant qu’il soit apaisiez;	And the treatment is that you should examine whether there is a hot abscess, and then put rosemary oil or chicken egg yolk on the spine until it is soothed;
puis met sus un des emplaustres confortans et sechans, et le lie d’un liien, et comande au malaide a reposer;	then place upon it one of the comforting and drying plasters, and tie it on with a bandage, and instruct the patient to rest.
et ne dorme mie sus celle partie ou il sent la dolor, tant k’il soit sanez.	and not to sleep on the painful part until he is healed.
Et se aucuns os se dessevre, si covient coper sus lou keur;	And if any bone protrudes, it must be covered with a bandage;
et oste l’os, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, a une costure, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if there is an open wound, then the two lips of the wound must be sutured together with thread, and then treated with ointment on a bandage until it heals;
et se li chiés de l’os est brisiez, ki est apelez li «chiés de la kowe», se i boute ton pouchet de ta main senestre, et le met igal a l’autre main a ton pooir, puis met l’emplaustre et l’estele sus, se tu en a mestier;	and if the shoulder of the bone is broken, which is called the 'shoulder blade', put your left hand's thumb into your mouth, and place it equally in your other hand to your power, then apply the plaster and bandage it up, if you need to;
puis l’estraint, et s’il i a os desevreit, si fent sus, et l’oste, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee.	then tighten it, and if there is a bone protruding, push it back in, take out the bone, and treat the wound until it is healed.
de la brisure de l’os de la hainche	of the fracture of the hip bone
Poc avient que li os de la hainche soit brisiez, et s’il avient, si n’avient fuer c’un poc d’amenuisement au chief;	Then it happens that the bones of the hip are broken, and if it happens, then there is a little lessening in the head.
et fent dou lonc, et decline au pardedens, et vient au malaide dolor au leu, et pointure, et enfle ceu que brise.	and they go long, and decline to the sides, and bring pain to the patient at the site, and piercing, and swelling in what is broken.
Et li restoration si est que tu estendes ta main sus, tant que tu soies sus la briseure;	And the restoration is that you extend your hand above it, as long as you are on the break;
et saiches quelz est li brisure et li figure de li;	and know which is the break and its shape;
et se li brisure est au chief soulement, si met igal cele brisure, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil.	and if the break is only in the head, then put it equal to that break, so that it is in its natural shape.Et s’il brise en la costure et en la fente, si leve li chiés soulement, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil;
Et se li brisure est dou lonc, ou elle decline au dedens, si fai gesir le malaide sus son ventre, tant que li restauration de cele brisure te soit aparillie.	And if the break is long, or it declines inward, then let the patient lie on his belly, so that the restoration of that break may be prepared for him.Et se ele est dou lonc et decline au pardedens, si met ele a figure de croisse; et li restauration de cele brisure est que tu le tiens sus, et qu’ele ne se mueve pas.
Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	And when you have made it equal, then put on the plaster, then put on a staff or kerchief, and constrict the break so that it does not move;
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	and apply the cautery under the ribs, so that the hair grows evenly.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	Instruct the patient to sleep on his healthy side or on his back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	And if an abscess comes out, do not touch it until the painful abscess is relieved, and put on what we have described before;
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	then return to the restoration, and tighten it as it should be, if there is no bad event;
et c’est li maniere.	and that is the way it is done.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	The shoulder joint is what is between the elbow and the head of the shoulder, and if it is dislocated, it should be restored according to one of two methods:Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals; et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	one of which is to take a thin staff, smooth and of middle thickness, according to this shape:Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	And take two ropes and tie them together, and hang the patient from above, and seat him on a chair;
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	then let him swing his broken arm down to the floor, and have a beam of wood inserted in it, then hang him from some heavy object so that he is stretched downward;
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	then have the helpers adjust the break to be even with his hands together, so that the break is set correctly.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a .ij. ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout .i. liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	And the other way is that one pins the patient to his hat, and ties his hand to his neck, then commands two ministers, one of whom presses what is on top of the fracture with his hands, and the other pulls from underneath to the end of the bond, and each stretches his part.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	And if you want the extraction to be more forceful, then compress beneath the fracture and above it, and extend each of the ministers to his part.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	And if the break is near the head of the shoulder, then you should place one rope in front under the armpit, and the other towards the neck, under the break;
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	and likewise if the break is towards the neck, then one rope should be placed lightly and gently, without effort, so that the break is set straight and on its proper place;Et se il ne voulent li chief de l’espaule demourer en son leu, si mets I liien legierement a lor col, et le remescheve vers la terre;
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	then make the cut even, as it should be, and hold it steady, if no abscess forms there.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	And if an abscess forms there, do not open it for seven days, but put soft lamb's wool soaked in arse and rose oil on it until the abscess is calm.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	Then open it, and the way to do this is to put the plaster on the cut, then raise the arm above the shoulder and put your hand on the shoulder or breast;
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	and press hard on the shoulder and arm so that the arm is straight, unless something else moves it or the bone has moved.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	And if you suspect the bone has moved, use splints and put a larger and stronger splint on the cut, with one inch of space between each splint, and make each splint large enough that it goes three inches beyond the cut on both sides.Et li esteles sont si fortes que elle ne se cassent mie;
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	then stretch them over the splints, as I said at the beginning of this chapter about fracture, harder and less by moving away.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if you see the position of the splints and the stretching, as we have said, in the hour that you restore the broken member, and you doubt the hot abscess, then leave it bound until the seventh day, as we have said.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	Then examine the binding every three days to ensure that itching or swelling does not occur in the area, and that the wound does not become too tight as it heals.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	If the wound, as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if no such accidents occur, then loosen the binding after three days or more, and let the patient sleep on his back with his hands on his stomach;
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	and place under the shoulder a pillow of equal wool, and check every hour of the day or night that the figure of the broken member does not move or the binding become soft;
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	if it is treated with medicine, and given the food we have previously mentioned, in such a way that the food reaches the uppermost subtleties.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	And when he begins to regain strength, then let him eat something substantial.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	It is usual for the shoulder and leg to take 40 days to heal completely;
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	and then one must loosen and administer baths and ointment treatments to ease the pain.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the dislocation is severe and stuck, it will take longer to loosen, up to two months.
de la brisure du bras	of the dislocation of the arm
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is made up of two bones, which are called the 'ulna', one of which is small and sits below the armpit.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	The other bone is larger and sits beneath the larger bone.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	Sometimes only the large bone is broken, sometimes only the small one, and sometimes both together.Si l’un est rompu et li autres entiers, li membres a devers la main doit estre tirrez et remuetz de son leu en tel maniere ke
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the small bones are broken, their restoration and healing is easy.
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	And when the large bones are broken, their healing is poor, and more difficult than when they are broken all at once.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If only the small bone is broken, then it should be put back into place gently and stretched slightly to align it. Se c’est li gros fosciles qui est brisié, si convient que tu le remes a son leu; et si il ne peut estre a son leu, si convient que tu le traies soulement en la guariçon, si com il est requerre.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	If it's a large bone, you must pull harder;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	and stretch him out on a pillow, and tie the hand pouch higher than the others, and the small fingers lower than the other fingers, and have the patient cross his legs over himself, and the pillow in front of him higher so that the patient doesn't have to exert any effort;
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	Then extend one minister's arm under his hand, or under his armpit, and another minister above him.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	And then the minister should apply pressure equally, according to the best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if there are pieces in the fracture, put each one in its place, and if none of them fit that poke the heart, and you cannot restore it to its place, then do as we said before, on the chest and the bone.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with the breaking there is a wound, I have spoken of it in a particular chapter;
si pren la cure.	then take the cure.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if, at the beginning of the restoration, suppurating ulcers appear, then apply a dressing of ceratum made from rose oil and white wax, neither too hard nor too soft.
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and leave the dressing in place gently, until the suppurating ulcers are soothed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	Then remove the ceratum, and apply an ointment made from flour with egg white, then put on the bandages, with the bandage for the fracture being a little stronger and a little larger than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	and know that there must be six bandages on the arm in various positions:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	whether the fracture is in one of the bones, or in two;
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	and tighten more over the fracture than elsewhere, and always less as time goes on, as I said at the beginning of this chapter;
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	and the bandages which are on the fracture be soft and moist, and not hard or rough;
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	and the thread, with which it is bound, of flax, nor too coarse nor too fine, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	And then remove the bandages and examine the limb and the fracture after a few days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if any bad accident happens to the member, such as itching coming to it, you must moisten the member with warm water until the itch is relieved;
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the member not be too tight or rest.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	And then begin the stretching again, and if the ligaments are relaxed and the bones displaced, and similarly, address it.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses .i. poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if one takes a bandage and the swelling cannot come to the member because it is too tight, then one must soften it a little and leave it for several days until the swelling goes down and then tighten it again.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things that we have said happen to the patient, then do not release him until 20 days.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	Or either he turns on his side, then he can put his hands to his neck, and let his necks be even, and guard against movement and rolling about, and sleep on his back;
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	and know that this fracture is restored in 30 days or 35, and perhaps in 20 days, according to the compositions and complexes of the virtues.
de la brisure de la main	of the fracture of the hand
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Know that in the back of the hand and on the knuckles there are few fractures, and only stretching occurs many times.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the palm of the hand is broken or folded, then the patient should sit cross-legged, and sit upright in front of him evenly;
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	then he should put his hand on the ground, and the minister should extend the broken bones, and make them equal so that they are well-joined;
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	and then put on the plaster and bandages, if no abscess comes, then he puts on a splint according to the quantity of the wound;et li minister li fait mettre sa main sus la toie estendue, et il tuit li met igalement. Et si li estele fu de grand leu, s’il mettret
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	and the minister makes him put his hand on the ground, and they all make it equal. And if the splint is of a large wound,
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the break is at the side of the palm around the belly, then make a ball of bandages, and instruct the patient to press it against his broken palm;et li ministers mette leu la spere et li estele en son leu, et li malaide l’estrainne tant qu’il soit bien igal.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	And then pull it with a long strap, and let the mark of the cautery be as big as the palm of your hand, and pull it, as it should be done.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is in the back of the hand, you must put a splint on top and another one underneath the palm so that the hand is open and straight, then tie it all around the hand, and stop the bleeding between the fingers.Et se li brisure est entre les dois, si covient que li malaide mette sa main croisie sus la brisure, et tu estaines lou liien entre les deux os brisiez, et lie tout entor la main; et se il y a grant flux de sang, si covient qu’il le frotte, si que li sang ne fluit.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the fracture is in one of our fingers, if it is the knuckle, set it straight, as it should be.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	And pull it with the palm, and if you see that a small, straight mark is placed to lift the fracture, and it does not move;
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	And if the fracture is in another finger, such as the index or another, set it straight and bind it to the healthy finger next to it;
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	Or you can bind them all together in a clench, or put a mark on it, as in the knuckle;
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	And take care in the restoration and the preparation of a hot abscess, and treat what comes out, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	of a broken thigh
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The bones of the thigh are often broken, and one can see this when it turns front and back.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and the healing is by binding above the fracture, and the other below.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	And the patient lies on his face, then each assistant extends their bandage to their side equally;
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	and this is when the fracture is in the middle of the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	And if the fracture is near the root of the thigh, then one ligament should go towards the buttock and the other below the fracture.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	And if it is near the knee, then the bandage should be above the knee, and the extension below;
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	then the surgeon sets the bone according to its natural shape with his two hands, and then applies the ointment and bandage, unless an abscess forms.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	And if there is a hot abscess, let it calm down, then return to your work and treatment;
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	the sling is made in this way.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	You should wrap the break with a hard bandage folded in two or three layers to stop the bleeding. Then turn the leg so that the heel comes to the root of the toe, and tie a long thread between the thigh and the leg, below the knee, so that the end of the thread comes above.
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then turn the bandage around the leg and thigh, and place splints on the break, and put a splint on the shinbone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then use eight pieces of soft cloth between the leg and thigh to make it even, and then start binding firmly in three or four turns around the break.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as you go higher up from the break, loosen the binding.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then cut two of the threads that you tied between the leg and thigh, and untie three splints that are above, then go back down to the end of the thread, so that you come under the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	and hold it, so that it does not move from its place, then leave it thus, until no abscess, swelling or similar occurs.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if something happens to it, then loosen it, and address what is happening to it, as we have said many times:
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	and if there are pieces of bone piercing through, then they must be removed, if possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	And if it cannot be removed, then the area should be split and the bone pulled out.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	And treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And sometimes the thighbone breaks in this way when they put on armor, just like in the shoulder and arm:
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	However, with this restoration, the malady is not relieved.Et si il ne se guérit, puis est grant douleur en li cuisse et en l’ajutoire, si
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en .l. jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And you should know that the hip is restored in one day, or a little less or more, according to the different constitutions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	of the joint of the knee
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	Know that in the knee joint there is little breaking, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is only a split, or a perforation, and it happens with any wound, and without a wound, and this feels good to everyone.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is to put straight what is bent in his fingers, so that when they are set straight he can move them.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	then apply the plaster, and put a round bandage on it if necessary, and bind it as it should be, then follow all the instructions we have given for other fractures, such as hot abscess and similar conditions;
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	applying to each injury what is suitable for it, until it is healed.
de la brisure de la jambe	of the fracture of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that in the leg there are two bones, of which one is properly called the 'tibia', and the other is called the 'fibula'.
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And it has all the same injuries as the arm, and its restoration is the same as that of the arm, and its treatment is also the same. And if both bones are broken together, then the leg becomes useless in every way.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if only the smaller bones are broken, then it turns forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the large bone is broken, one feels great pain, and it is seen clearly;
et torne desoz.	and turns underneath.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Therefore, apply extension, and make it equal, and tie the bandages equally;
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	but if the break is ugly, and there are several pieces, then the extension should be less and gentler;
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	and adjust it according to your skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have finished your work, take two bundles of wooden splints that reach from one side of the leg to the other, and let them be as long as the leg from just below the knee to beneath the foot;
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	then wrap two bands around them above and below, and tie it in the middle as well, and at this time, the leg will not be able to decline to the right or left, and thus it is good;
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	and some administer the fire cautery on the long bone of the leg, and it is from the wood, and they put the leg forward to prevent movement, and properly they do this in the break where there is injury;
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	and move the leg each day, to see if there is any hot abscess or other accident;
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	until it is healed.
de la brisure des os dou piet	of the break in the bones of the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle there is no break, but sometimes there is a break in the bones of the foot and also two wounds, and it happens with various injuries.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there is a broken bone in the foot, and you see the bones protruding on top of each other, then put the patient's foot down on the ground, as if he wanted to walk, and then put your own foot on his, where the bones are raised, and then press it until they return to their place;
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then put on the ointment and bandages, and under the sole of the foot place a small wooden board with two flat sides, then tighten it to the foot comfortably, then wrap cloth around it, and other things that you need.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And after three or four days have passed, loosen the bandage, for you will find the bones healed, whether broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if any of the fingers are broken, restore them, as we have said for the fingers of the hand;
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	then put a splint on the broken finger according to its length, and let it be a little wider, then place under the foot that table which I have described, and adjust it properly.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	and if there are two or three, or more, broken, then put on each finger a splint according to its size, wrapped in a linen cloth, and adjust the table under the foot.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	and let there be a stop under the head of the table pressing against the belly of the foot, so that it may hold well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And you must not forget the other things I have said about other fractures, for which we have already spoken:
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	and treat each accident as it should be treated.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	of the fracture of the bone in the wrist
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bones of nature are broken, let her sit upright, then lean towards the back, and be held from behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the hollow with cotton wool, and put in as much as it can hold.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then raise the woman, and gently press her back little by little, and thus the cotton will go into the hollow, and the bones with it.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she needs to urinate, remove the cotton, and when she has finished, put it back again. Do this for seven days.
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	The fracture will then be healed, and if you wish, take a bladder of a ram, tie it at the neck with a string, and fill the bladder with the hollow.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	Then blow into the string until the bladder is inflated inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	nature will heal the fracture
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then it should be filled with cotton, and left like that for several days, until it heals.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the bone of the man's or woman's shoulder is broken, we restore it in the same way as we have said about the hip bone;
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	and these breaks are not hidden from those who dedicate themselves to studying and understanding my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the break reveals in many ways the correct path to restoration:
enten le donques.	listen therefore.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	When a rod is broken, take a goose's throat and insert the rod into it;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	then wrap cloth around it, leave it for three days or tie it tightly, and it will heal quickly.
de brisure avec plaie	from breaking with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for one who has a break with a wound, especially if it is large, such as in the thigh or shoulder bone or similar, to be treated immediately, as the remedies we have described attest.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, and there is no infection from vitriol, if you have nothing else, then restart by resetting the dislocation in that same hour, or that day, if no abscesses arise.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	And if a hot abscess comes, let recovery wait until the next day, so that the abscess may be quieted; and don't touch it on the third or fourth day, for you would bring about an evil accident.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone is appearing on the uncovered chest, one should gently put it back into place with slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extension is not available to make your hands even, then use this instrument which is made of iron, seven or eight inches long, and its width according to the size of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and therefore it is necessary for the surgeon to have three or four, depending on what he needs for each fracture treatment.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and it should be round and slightly large so that it does not bend when compressed on the limb while you work, and it should be pointed at the front, and thick in the middle towards the front, like this:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	And it is called a "spit", so that the curved head should be placed on the prominent part of the bone;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and the handle at another time, as much as it will go, and it should be even with each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the dislocation is subtle, and the instrument cannot hold the bone well, then you must chip the head of the bone, so that the instrument can hold it.Et si li brisure est griez, et le chef de l’os est trove par la pelezure del chiés, si covient que tu ramones la dislocation premierement; car il n’est pas bon qu’il soit contusioné en pluxors lieux.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reset the bone as we have said, then use an appropriate tool, such as an incision knife or needle, at your discretion;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then cut away what is left in the bone of asperities and fine splinters.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset and the patient feels great pain afterwards, know that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Do this until it is in its place, then moisten the cloth with black sticky wine, and properly if it is in a wound.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not put cerotic ointment or anything else on the wound that would cause pus and corruption;
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	then dress the wound once you have set the bone, and leave the wound uncovered, and bandage it all around according to the size of the wound, and take care that the wound is not constricted by the bandage;
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	and many times this has been done to fools, causing pain, or sometimes death or corrosion;
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and it is the most gentle and effective treatment for dislocation.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is large or deep, and you doubt that a bad accident will occur as we have said, and you feel pain in the area, then you should not put anything on it;
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	but wrap around, instead of pillows, hard, folded cloths, and tie them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see after one or two days that pus is coming from the wound, then remove what you have put on it and put on an ointment that heals wounds, such as tetrafarmaçon and similar ointments.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	And when the bone is back in its natural place, it should be made comfortable and not restricted; and if there are great pains, anoint with healing oil or ointment by rubbing, such as oil of larkspur, or of laurier, or of garlic, or of onions, or of other healing oils.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is necessary for the limb to be prepared in such a way that the bowstring runs downstream easily.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if they persist for many days and the bow cannot be set but keeps slipping back, know that there are tiny pieces of bone causing this, so you must probe the wound with a probe, and remove all these broken pieces that cause the pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula or other form of corruption occurs, you should treat it according to what he said in the chapter above.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and open on the limb, as in the thigh or shoulder bone, and similar large bones, do not draw it out, but leave it be until it can be pulled out;
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	by chance it will fall out after 20 or 30 days, then clean the wound if you can;
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	and if you cannot, then leave it be.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	of bruises that come over the soudure
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	Many times after the healing of the fracture, especially when it is near the joint, it is an ugly sight to see the shape of the limb;
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	and by chance the limb cannot do its natural works.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	So be wary then if the nerve is affected:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	if the patient takes constipating medicines such as aloes, incense, myrrh, and sarcocolla, aconite, and similar others, either by themselves or all together, and concocts them with dry wine, egg white, or garlic;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and places them on the head as poultices, pressing firmly, and not loosening for several days.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	and then he loosens it, and begins another one, until the swelling is gone;
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	or you press on a well-made plaster;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	for the property of the plaster is that it removes all swellings from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	and if the swelling has turned into a hardness like stone, and it needs to be removed, cut away the top, and reveal the excess;
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	or you have it removed by a shaver, until it is gone, and then dress the wound until it heals.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	of the limb which is weakened after healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the broken bone is restored, and remains weak and slender after the limb, this happens for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	one of which is that it was bound too tightly, and not as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there are too many ligaments, and the nourishment cannot reach the member;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or for excess of moisture;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or for too great movement, not in its hour;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because there is little blood in his body, and he is weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is that you feed the patient and make the body tender, so that the blood increases within him;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and give him baths, and give him joy and leisure;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	then apply pitch to the limb so that it attracts great nourishment, and often bathe it in warm water, until the nourishment reaches the limb;Et li cure si est qu’il soit mene a la chause, et al buef, et a la vine, et a la lieure, et a la seliere, et au vin clers, et a l’ole, et a la migaie, et aux fraies, et au pain d’
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	And the treatment is that he be led to walk, and ride a horse, and go hunting, and play sports,
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	until the limb is straightened after health
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the broken bones are visible, and the form of the limb is ugly, nevertheless it does not lose its natural function.
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	don't believe the fools who say that one must break the limb again from scratch, and many foolish people have done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and these practices are blamed, and they cause great harm and sometimes death;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	nevertheless, if the dislocations and the tortures are recent, then they should be soaked in hot water or herbs that soften, such as leaves of marsh-mallow, roots, and sweet rocket, and similar things;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and make a soothing ointment from diaquilon, and take the mucilage of marsh-mallow, and cook it with tallow or sesame oil, and apply it to the affected area;
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or you take fat figs and grind them with horse manure, and similar medicines that soften quickly.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes the dislocation is caused by continuous and prolonged rubbing with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And bring about movement in the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the twist is awake and hardened like stone, and it needs to be removed with iron, then it must be cut close to the bone, with a thin, delicate incision.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and put poultice and bandage in the treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs in someone, one must immediately bring it back into alignment without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if it is delayed, the place will swell, and perhaps it will be reset in the wrong position;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	Therefore, one should not move it when it is swollen:
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	many times it brings spasms and other pains;li corps ne puet demorer en leus, ains doit il se mouevoir.
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	Nevertheless, when this happens, the patient should be bled, then left alone until the abscesses are soothed;et li dolors et les spames, et li moevemens, si conviennent qu’il demoure en leus.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	then warm the limb with hot water and oil, then reset it gently, and treat each limb as the healing comes into its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters on dislocation from the head to the feet.
des mandibules	of the jaws
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	It happens that jaws are dislocated downward, and dislocations of both are according to two manners:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	either they are slightly displaced from their places, and softened a little;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	or they are completely displaced and hang down; saliva flows from his mouth which he cannot hold, nor can he close his mouth or wrap his tongue around words.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When the dislocation is small, it returns by itself in several ways.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is complete and accomplished, then you must reset it quickly and not delay at all;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a way that the minister grabs the head of the patient, and pushes his fingers of one hand into the root of the jaw's joint inside the mouth, if the dislocation is on both sides;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other two fingers of the hand should be pressed down to straighten them;
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and instruct the patient to soften his jaw, and move it all around.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And the priest looks at her equally, until she returns to her place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if they are stuck together, especially if it is the two mandibles, pour hot water and oil over them, moving them gently;
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	do not force them, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are returned to their proper position and the mouth of the patient is closed properly without softening, then place wet cloths on it made from rose oil and wax, then tie it lightly with soft bindings;
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	and let the patient sleep on his back, and let his head be between two pillows so that he does not move it to the right or left, nor try to speak, but take light food, until the pain is gone, and the jaw joint is healed;
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	and then eat and drink what he wants easily, without opening his mouth to chew or drink, until the jaw is well healed and healthy.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be reset within an hour and are not converted to their places, then fevers and usual sores come, and perhaps stomach issues, and perhaps vomiting pure bile.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, then you will know it is destruction:
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times the person dies within seven days.
de la forcelle	of the fork
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The forepaw cannot be dislocated from within the continued part of it and from the foot, and is dislocated sometimes by force, and it is felt well.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	The cure is for the patient to lie flat on his back and extend his arms:
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press firmly on the spot with your palm, and it will return to its place;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then apply the ointment and bandage it tightly;
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the shoulder that is towards the neck cannot be dislocated;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it dislocates even once, then reset it to its place, as we have said;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply the ointment and bandage it tightly, and instruct the patient to rest until he is healed;
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	and thus is the head of the shoulder brought back when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	of shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	You should know that there are three ways in which the shoulder can be dislocated:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	One way is for it to dislocate at the bottom part of the shoulder;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	And the second way is at the top of the foot;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	And by chance it dislocates from above, and that rarely happens;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	It does not dislocate behind the shoulder, nor inside for the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	And often it dislocates underneath towards the shoulder, especially in those who are very thin, because in them it comes out easily;
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	In those who are fat, it only comes out and goes back in with force.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And by chance it happens to some men that they receive a blow or bruise, and the shoulder swells with a hot abscess, and they think it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore you must test it to make sure;de coi si ele desalue par la partie dou pis, et ne se remue point, sache bien qu’ele est desaluee a li asselle, et sache qu’
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And you will know of a dislocation when it is lower towards the armpit, and there is a difference between the sick shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find between them a manifest difference;
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find a pit at the top of the shoulder, and under the armpit the top of the shoulder as though it were an egg;
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring their hand to their nose, nor move in any way;
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and also, if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden, for you will find it clearly at the top;
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	and this type of dislocation is not difficult to fix when it is new, or if the child is sick.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the method is for the assistant to lift the hand of the sick person up, then put your knees under the armpit and lift the joint with force upwards into place;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and the minister lifts the hand, then extends it upward, before placing it back down.
si venra hastanment.	then come quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come as we have said within a few days, then the patient should be bathed in warm water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the minister should apply softening and soothing poultices, such as infusions of alder, fenugreek, and cornflower in water, and it should be applied;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then the patient should be laid on his back, and a woolen cloth of equal thickness, neither too soft nor too hard, should be placed underneath him. Then the minister should place his heel on the sto, and lift the head of the shoulder gently, and draw the hand of the patient;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and another minister should hold the head of the patient, so that it does not move downward;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	that shoulder returns right away, and if you set it again according to this method:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and you should have a person present who is larger than the patient;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and should stand straight toward the shoulder, and push his shoulder under the armpit of the patient, and lift the armpit upward, so that the patient hangs in the air;
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	and another assistant pulls the hand of the patient downward toward the belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the disease is too slight, one can place something heavy on it, and the dislocation will return immediately.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	And it is reset in another way:Tu prends la main dou malaides, et mets li doigt sus li col, et
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	and you put your finger on his neck, and you push the long brand into the ground so that the shoulder is as high as the wrist, neither too thick nor too thin;
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then it is placed under the patient, but he should have a soft cloth over him, and the patient should be still from the waist up;
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	then let his hand be stretched out downwards on the other side, and the joint will return to its place gently;
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if it does not want to return despite all that we have said, then perform this cure:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take a stick two arms long and four digits wide, with the tip bent backwards to fit into the joint beneath the dislocation, as follows:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	then tie it with a cloth under the joint of the patient so that the stick does not hurt him, then put it underneath the dislocation:
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	and stretch out his arm over the long stick and tie the shoulder to the stick, and the arm to the tip of the hand, then put his arm on the edge of a board that is wider than it is long, and stretch out his hand downwards, and let the body hang down on the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	the joint returns now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is back in place, however it is, you should put a sphere of wool under the shoulder blade, then apply the prepared ointment made from mill dust, with incense and egg white, over the entire shoulder and around it; then stretch it underneath the shoulder blade gently, and tie the string over the ointment, and embrace the hand to his chest, and let the arm remain like this.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And one must eat little, as long as the member is comfortable, for it will heal faster.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	and then eat more after a few days or seven, and move it;
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	and if it is stiff and not soft, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint has left its place due to moisture or for any other reason, you should administer cauteries to it at three openings, as described in the chapter on cauteries.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all this and it comes undone after seven days, and the joint does not hold, and he cannot lift his arm upstream, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is cut or stretched out or softened;
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and know that the joint will never be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation which is towards the foot, and of the breast, or behind, is made by thrusting, and stretching with the hands, and one administers to another;
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing there is pain in the limb, and with movement it becomes worse over time, then the patient should use the bath many times until the pain goes away and returns to its original nature.
de la dislocation dou coute	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the joint of the neck is dislocated at times, and returns to place.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	and is dislocated in all parts, especially in front and behind; the dislocation is not reset, for it can be seen and felt.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	and it dislocates according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick neck with the healthy one, you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	Because the joint is damaged and cannot bend the arm or touch its shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you must reset it as you would an abscess, for if a deep abscess comes, it would be painful to reset.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and at times it cannot be fully reset, especially when it is in the back;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	it is worse than other dislocations and causes greater pain, and sometimes death ensues.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And when it can be reset, you must extend your arm with both hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	and his arms should be spread out, and the hands turned according to the neck, all around, and the joint pressed at its joints together, or at the root of the palm, until it returns to place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, then it returns when he bends his hand to his hand, and raises from the root of the palm the wrist which was dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to go back into place, then apply strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and one minister extends the arm, and the other tilts it, so that it does not move with the extension;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm to each side after you have wrapped a long, wide cloth around it;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when you see the joint of the hand, anoint it with oil to soften the joint, then push the joint firmly back into place;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is back in place, apply a dry plaster with egg white, and hold it firmly, and wind the arm around the neck of the patient, and leave it for several days, then remove the plaster.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firm in its place, then loosen the binding, and leave it;
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	and if you see that the joint is not set well, then start over with the plaster and binding, and leave it for several days until it is firmly in place;
puis le deslie.	then loosen it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if he feels pain after the joint is moved back into place, and it still moves, then bathe and rub it gently, and press until the pain subsides.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	Or you may place a fat sheep's testicle on the joint, then leave it for a day and night, then remove it, and have him enter the bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when he sweats, gently rub the joint, then put the testicle back on, and then back into the bath. And so do this repeatedly until the pain is gone.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do this two or three times, until he is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see that it is moist, put warm cow manure on it with butter and press it onto the joint;
