si revenra a sa disposition.	and it will return to its natural state.
li dislocation de la main	dislocations of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	A dislocated hand is healing, and the recovery is quicker than for other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it is necessary to return it to its place gradually, at the same time that it was dislocated, so that the joint swells or a hot abscess forms there.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the method of reduction is to place the patient's hand on a table, and extend the minister's hand, and look at it placed evenly so that he places his palm over the appearance of the joint, and push it until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you should check that it is in the right place;
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	then put the patient's back of his hand on a table, extended and reduced.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	If the dislocation is at the back of the hand, then put the patient's hand on a table with his palm facing upwards, and let the assistant put his hand on the affected joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, that is good.S’ele ne veut revenir, mettes li la main sus une tauble,
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, then strain with soothing plasters hot abscesses, and leave it thus without re-encasing.Et s’il li traist au leu, si li mettiez une fons de vinas a la jointure et al oile de panon, et al oile d’olifre, ou
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you cannot put it back in place after a few days, then the joint will remain crooked.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and does no harm to the patient as long as the hand is soft and can grasp nothing at all:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then you know that the nerves are cut, or the arteries;
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is nothing else to do except to cauterize the area, and perhaps nothing else will help.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, then apply the plaster that we have mentioned, then constrict it and leave it for 5 days, then loosen it and let it be thus.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he cannot move it well, and there is any swelling, then moisten it with warm water, and rub it until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	of the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Sometimes the fingers of the hand are dislocated on both sides, sometimes at the back of the palm or on the inside;
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	then reset the fingers, and pull them back into place until they are aligned, then hold the top of the finger, and turn it towards the affected part;
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and let it be for two days, and then put it back in place that same day;
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and do not eat at night as we have said, but during the day, make him move and then put him to bed.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this often, until he is healed, and also do the same if he is dislocated in his hand or arm, and act just as before, until he is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and do the same for any other dislocation.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	from the dislocation of the head and back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the head or neck is dislocated, there is no cure, for death comes quickly with this ailment.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs are that the bowels move without willing it, and he cannot hold it back, and often a member becomes paralyzed, either both legs or both arms or one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the skin becomes black in four places:
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	the one that turns black on the back is called "gilbositez":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	the treatment for this is to reward if the blackness comes from childhood.
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	if there is no cure or healing, no matter what.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or from blows or similar things, the ancients spoke of many ways to cure with great words, but in all cases there was not much benefit;
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	but I have abbreviated it according to my intention, and formed instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that the hunchback that comes before the foot, neither medicine nor health heals;
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	and also that which comes directly on both sides, and cannot be healed except by that which comes properly in the back, as I said;
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	and it is that the disease be stretched out on his face in one place equally, and have a strap under him, so that he does not bend;
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	then insert the brand into the head on the ground firmly, and another at the feet, and tie a string under the armpits of the disease, and another at the hips, and at the knees, and at the ankles;
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and two servants know the bonds, one at the head and the others at the feet, among the twelve torches;
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and let them be well bound, the torches as we have said, and let the nurse put her palms on the spine, until it straightens out.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not straighten out with this treatment, take a board three yards long, and lay it under the back, and let the patient lie on his side, and put the middle of the board under the spine;
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and let the nurse put her feet on the other end of the board, and press firmly, until it straightens out;
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you see it, turn the wheel that turns to the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And it is that you fix two torches at the head of the patient's arm, and two others towards the feet, and have between each torch, above and below, a palm of space;
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and have a hole in each stake where the cord runs through, and let the stakes be firmly driven into the ground so that they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each pair of stakes have a turning stake, around which the cords turn, and at each turning place have two small stakes about a palm long for the cord to turn around.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	Then tie the cord that is between the stakes at the head to the turning stake towards the head, and the other cord towards the feet to the other turning stake, and each of the ministers turns their turning stake along all the cord, and the master puts the spine level as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is level, then put on a drying plaster with an abundance of egg white, and then the bandages, and then the pillow of a tablet three digits long, so that it covers the hunchback area and the healthy part of the spine, then bind it with a cord as we have said, and use the patient's subtle numbing medicine until they are healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if nothing comes of it for the health, then one must administer softening and soothing medicines, with the star that we mentioned earlier;
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and sometimes they administer a poultice, and sometimes the appearance comes in the lower spine of the back, and one thinks it is dislocation;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and it is the bone that is exposed, therefore one must not be too presumptuous about it:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	for fear of causing death.
des dislocations de la hainche	of hip dislocations
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	You should know that in the joints of the hip and the shoulder, there are no dislocations, only in the other joints; and there is no dislocation like those others;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the joint of the hip is dislocated into four parts:d’une part li os qui est a la cote, et li os qui est a la cuisse, et li os qui est a
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	one part is the bone that is at the ribcage, and the bone that is at the thigh, and the bone that is inside
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more inside, and little dislocated before and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation inside is that when one joins the affected leg with the healthy one, it is longer, and the affected knee appears more open than the healthy one, and the affected person cannot bend their knee to the fire.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and the area near it is swollen with a hot abscess due to the shoulder joint coming closer.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him to whom it comes from without, is that this accident is contrary to those before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of someone who has this in front are that their leg is well aligned according to its structure.
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	However, they cannot bend their knee without pain, and if they want to walk, they cannot do so, and they retain their urine, and the ankle swells, and when they go to the toilet, they pass it over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him to whom it happens behind, are that he cannot bend or double his knee, and that leg is more crooked than the other, and the veins are softened, and the head of the thigh is at the place below the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The cause of this type of dislocation is that you first check if the dislocation is old and it remains in its position, then there will be no improvement.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and he must not become presumptuous.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And for those with a fresh dislocation, which comes in three ways, you must hurry to return the joint to its place, and stretch it in and out, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	Perhaps it will return on its own and not need further treatment.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this way, you must strongly pull the limb, and hold the leg firmly with two hands, or with one hand tied to the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and another person stretches their hand over it in such a way that they push their hands under their armpits, then tightens a cord around the thigh;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and another ties the head;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and they all pull up and down at the same time, until the patient is lifted off the ground once, and then hold him suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This stretching method is common for four appearances, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then treatment must be applied to its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the armpit, you must lead the patient to lie on his healthy side, then place the ligature at the root of the thigh, and at the spot below the armpit, then let the ligature ascend towards the armpit and the axilla;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then have another assistant grip his arms and squeeze and extend the affected thigh in a correct manner:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	and if it does not return to its place immediately;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this type of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot bring it back in the manner we have described, then you must tie together both feet of the patient with a strong, soft ligature around the heels and knees, and have the affected leg extended two fingers more than the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then let him be hung from the top of a pole, and let him be two arms' length above the ground;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	then instruct the assistant to hold the top of the thigh tightly, and another assistant hanging with the patient should hold the thigh firmly, for the joint will return quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is healed, then let the patient lie down, as we have said in the case of gout, and tightly bind the leg and foot that has been affected;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then put two torches on, one at the head and one at the foot, then place the torch between the legs of the patient in the dislocation;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and have wet cloths laid all around so that the patient does not blush, then each assistant stretches him towards themself, and the examiner puts pressure with his hand on the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	Otherwise, place him on a table and press it as we have said in the case of dislocation, and lay the patient on his healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when a dislocation is in front, then the leg of the patient must be extended gently, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and places his weight upon the affected angle, then presses with the other hand, and stretches it downward towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is to the rear, then the patient should not be stretched out downward, nor lifted up off the ground, but he must be as though his hip were dislocated to the rear, just as we have said about lying on one's side with both hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and it is on his face, and the bandage stretched as we have said before, and one must press on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be in place when the patient stretches his legs, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then adjust the thighs, and apply the ointment, and restrain it with a bandage so that the hip does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and rest for 3 or 4 days, then loosen it, and apply the ointment on top of it;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, then restrain them as before, and leave it for 3 days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then loosen it, and make him walk comfortably until the limb is healed.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee is dislocated in 3 ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is, inside and outside, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not give up.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you command the patient to bend his leg at the thigh, and if it does not straighten at the thigh, know that he is dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and place your back against his face, and put his foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take his knee in your palms, and pull between your fingers, then bend both sides of the knee jointly;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and another minister extends his foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he straightens his leg at the thigh easily;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and put on the plaster, and straighten the leg at the thigh, and bind them together strongly for 3 or 4 days, then loosen it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not move the patient until the limb is conforted.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the member is not at all, then administer strong stretching, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes dislocated, and sometimes fully relaxed, both inside and out.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and lean forward towards the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the movements should be light, and one should gently extend the hand when it is only numbed.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is dislocated all the way through, you should make the patient sit upright, and hold the limb firmly by the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then with the left twice, then extend it upwards, and flex it gently upwards;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, by bending and pulling the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns to place, that is good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, then perform the action again, for it will return;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot be reset in that way, then make the patient lie on his back on the ground and push the staff firmly into the ground between his buttocks, and tie a cloth around him so that he does not bend forward.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then the assistant pulls on the thigh, while another assistant stretches out the foot with his hands or with a rope tied around the ankle, holding it against the collar of the leg.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then each assistant pulls equally, and the staff is placed between the buttocks of the patient to restrain him when they stretch.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then the assistants put their weight into their hands, and another assistant pulls on the healthy leg from below, and the dislocation will return with force.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is back in place, then apply the plaster and bandages on top, and pull it firmly, and tie the foot to the leg, and be careful of the nerves that are on the ankle behind, so that the ligature is not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then let it stay for two or three days, and if the ligatures loosen, then tighten them again;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then untie it on the third or fourth day, and the patient can go about their business after four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if he goes before that time, it is not safe for him to do so, as he may relapse.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if painful abscesses arise, then you must soothe them as we have said elsewhere, until they heal.
des dois	of the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the arms are dislocated, one should stretch them gently without force, and this is a minor issue.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any part of the back or foot, you should have the patient sit upright on a flat surface or table, then put your foot over the affected area and press down firmly until it pops back into place;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is back in place and there is nothing protruding, put a two-footed board under the sole of the foot, then tighten it firmly, and leave it for three days, then untie it;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let him rest until he is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with dislocation, and one wishes to restore it, many times the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not presumptuous in the treatment, if you are wise in the art and have used it for a long time, and if you are pitying and merciful and slow to anger; then do not be bold.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and in the beginning, use things that soothe an abscess, and leave the patient in God's hand if you do not see hope of health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then immediately reset the member to its place so that the hot abscesses heal.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the member is in its place, then minister soothing things for hot abscesses and treat the wound as it should be with drying ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if there is a fracture along with the dislocation and broken small bones, then set the bones, and do what we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and beware of going astray out of fear, according to what I have said, for it is better for you according to your Creator, and for the safety of your weapons and your body.
